code = """#!/usr/bin/env python3
\"\"\"
baWithPathModel.py

CLI wrapper around the Ceres backend (mouse_ba) using a Python front-end.
- Reads cameras.json, mouse template (.txt), and dlc_long.csv
- Initializes poses from multi-view triangulation
- Runs model-based BA with soft spline (path) priors + rigid template + tiny slack offsets
- Writes estimated 3D body-part coordinates in coords_3d.csv format
- Optionally compares against ground-truth coords_3d.csv and prints accuracy stats

Place this script in the `python/` folder (next to frontend.py), or adjust imports accordingly.
\"\"\"

from __future__ import annotations

import argparse
import sys
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, Tuple, List, Optional

import numpy as np
import pandas as pd


def _auto_add_build_to_syspath() -> None:
    \"\"\"Make 'import mouse_ba' work without requiring PYTHONPATH.\"\"\"
    script_dir = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
    build_dir = script_dir.parent / "build"
    if build_dir.exists():
        sys.path.insert(0, str(build_dir))


_auto_add_build_to_syspath()

# Local front-end helpers (from your project)
from frontend import (
    load_cameras_json,
    load_dlc_long_csv,
    init_poses_from_triangulation,
    default_weight_pack,
)

import mouse_ba


def load_template_names_points(path: str | Path) -> Tuple[List[str], np.ndarray]:
    \"\"\"Read template file; returns (names, pts[J,3]).\"\"\"
    path = Path(path)
    names: List[str] = []
    pts: List[List[float]] = []
    with path.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for line in f:
            s = line.strip()
            if not s:
                break
            parts = s.split()
            if len(parts) != 4:
                break
            name = parts[0]
            try:
                x, y, z = float(parts[1]), float(parts[2]), float(parts[3])
            except ValueError:
                break
            names.append(name)
            pts.append([x, y, z])
    if not names:
        raise ValueError(f"Template file {path} did not contain a '<name> x y z' block.")
    return names, np.asarray(pts, dtype=np.float64)


def quat_normalize(q: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
    n = np.linalg.norm(q, axis=-1, keepdims=True)
    n = np.where(n == 0.0, 1.0, n)
    return q / n


def quat_to_rotmat_wxyz(q: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
    \"\"\"q: (...,4) in (w,x,y,z). returns (...,3,3).\"\"\"
    q = quat_normalize(q)
    w, x, y, z = q[..., 0], q[..., 1], q[..., 2], q[..., 3]
    ww, xx, yy, zz = w*w, x*x, y*y, z*z
    wx, wy, wz = w*x, w*y, w*z
    xy, xz, yz = x*y, x*z, y*z

    R = np.empty(q.shape[:-1] + (3, 3), dtype=np.float64)
    R[..., 0, 0] = ww + xx - yy - zz
    R[..., 0, 1] = 2.0 * (xy - wz)
    R[..., 0, 2] = 2.0 * (xz + wy)

    R[..., 1, 0] = 2.0 * (xy + wz)
    R[..., 1, 1] = ww - xx + yy - zz
    R[..., 1, 2] = 2.0 * (yz - wx)

    R[..., 2, 0] = 2.0 * (xz - wy)
    R[..., 2, 1] = 2.0 * (yz + wx)
    R[..., 2, 2] = ww - xx - yy + zz
    return R


def build_estimated_coords_df(
    joint_names: List[str],
    template_pts: np.ndarray,
    mouse_quat: np.ndarray,
    mouse_trans: np.ndarray,
    slack: np.ndarray,
    fps: float,
    behavior_default: int = 0,
) -> pd.DataFrame:
    \"\"\"Return DataFrame in coords_3d.csv format.\"\"\"
    M, T, J, _ = slack.shape
    assert template_pts.shape == (J, 3)

    R = quat_to_rotmat_wxyz(mouse_quat)  # (M,T,3,3)
    local = template_pts[None, None, :, :] + slack  # (M,T,J,3)
    world = (R[..., None, :, :] @ local[..., None]).squeeze(-1) + mouse_trans[..., None, :]

    frames = np.arange(T, dtype=np.int32)
    times = frames.astype(np.float64) / float(fps)

    recs = []
    for m in range(M):
        for t in range(T):
            for j in range(J):
                recs.append((
                    int(frames[t]),
                    float(times[t]),
                    int(m),
                    int(behavior_default),
                    joint_names[j],
                    float(world[m, t, j, 0]),
                    float(world[m, t, j, 1]),
                    float(world[m, t, j, 2]),
                ))
    return pd.DataFrame(recs, columns=["frame", "time", "mouse_id", "behavior", "node", "x", "y", "z"])


def compare_to_ground_truth(est_df: pd.DataFrame, gt_path: str | Path) -> Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]:
    \"\"\"Compare estimates to coords_3d.csv ground truth; returns summary tables.\"\"\"
    gt_df = pd.read_csv(gt_path)
    required = {"frame", "mouse_id", "node", "x", "y", "z"}
    missing = required - set(gt_df.columns)
    if missing:
        raise ValueError(f"Ground truth file missing required columns: {sorted(missing)}")

    keys = ["frame", "mouse_id", "node"]
    m = est_df.merge(gt_df[keys + ["x", "y", "z"]], on=keys, suffixes=("_est", "_gt"), how="inner")
    if len(m) == 0:
        raise ValueError("No matching rows between estimate and ground truth (check node names / frame count).")

    dx = m["x_est"].to_numpy() - m["x_gt"].to_numpy()
    dy = m["y_est"].to_numpy() - m["y_gt"].to_numpy()
    dz = m["z_est"].to_numpy() - m["z_gt"].to_numpy()
    err = np.sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy + dz*dz)
    m["err_mm"] = err

    overall = pd.DataFrame([{
        "N": int(len(err)),
        "RMSE_mm": float(np.sqrt(np.mean(err**2))),
        "MAE_mm": float(np.mean(np.abs(err))),
        "Median_mm": float(np.median(err)),
        "P95_mm": float(np.percentile(err, 95)),
        "P99_mm": float(np.percentile(err, 99)),
    }])

    per_node = (
        m.groupby("node")["err_mm"]
         .agg(
             N="count",
             RMSE_mm=lambda x: float(np.sqrt(np.mean(np.square(x)))),
             MAE_mm="mean",
             Median_mm="median",
             P95_mm=lambda x: float(np.percentile(x, 95)),
         )
         .reset_index()
         .sort_values("RMSE_mm", ascending=False)
    )

    per_mouse = (
        m.groupby("mouse_id")["err_mm"]
         .agg(
             N="count",
             RMSE_mm=lambda x: float(np.sqrt(np.mean(np.square(x)))),
             MAE_mm="mean",
             Median_mm="median",
             P95_mm=lambda x: float(np.percentile(x, 95)),
         )
         .reset_index()
         .sort_values("mouse_id")
    )

    return {"overall": overall, "per_node": per_node, "per_mouse": per_mouse, "merged": m}


def build_arg_parser() -> argparse.ArgumentParser:
    p = argparse.ArgumentParser(
        prog="baWithPathModel.py",
        description="Model-based BA with soft spline priors + rigid template + tiny slack offsets.",
    )
    p.add_argument("--cameras", required=True, help="Path to cameras.json")
    p.add_argument("--template", required=True, help="Path to mouse template file (e.g., mouse3_mesh_shortTail.txt)")
    p.add_argument("--dlc", required=True, help="Path to DLC long-format CSV (dlc_long.csv)")
    p.add_argument("--fps", type=float, default=10.0, help="Frames per second (default: 10)")
    p.add_argument("--out", required=True, help="Output CSV path for estimated 3D coordinates (coords_3d.csv format)")
    p.add_argument("--gt", default=None, help="Optional ground-truth coords_3d.csv to compare against")

    p.add_argument("--init-likelihood-min", type=float, default=0.2,
                   help="Likelihood threshold for triangulation-based initialization (default: 0.2)")

    p.add_argument("--max-iter", type=int, default=200, help="Ceres max iterations (default: 200)")
    p.add_argument("--threads", type=int, default=8, help="Ceres threads (default: 8)")
    p.add_argument("--verbose", action="store_true", help="Print Ceres iteration table")
    p.add_argument("--optimize-cameras", action="store_true", help="Estimate camera extrinsics (default off)")
    p.add_argument("--optimize-intrinsics", action="store_true", help="Estimate camera intrinsics (default off)")

    # Ablation-ish toggles (no backend changes required)
    p.add_argument("--disable-path", action="store_true",
                   help="Disable spline/path priors by setting their weights ~0.")
    p.add_argument("--rigid-only", action="store_true",
                   help="Force slack offsets ~0 (pure rigid template).")

    return p


def main() -> int:
    args = build_arg_parser().parse_args()

    cam_quat, cam_trans, cam_intr = load_cameras_json(args.cameras)
    joint_names, template_pts = load_template_names_points(args.template)

    (obs_cam, obs_mouse, obs_joint, obs_frame,
     obs_x, obs_y, obs_l, num_frames) = load_dlc_long_csv(args.dlc)

    init_q, init_t = init_poses_from_triangulation(
        template_pts,
        obs_cam, obs_mouse, obs_joint, obs_frame, obs_x, obs_y, obs_l,
        cam_quat, cam_trans, cam_intr,
        likelihood_min=args.init_likelihood_min,
    )

    wp = default_weight_pack().to_dict()

    # knot interval ≈ 0.3s worth of frames, min 3
    wp["knot_interval_frames"] = max(3, int(round(args.fps * 0.3)))

    if args.disable_path:
        wp["sigma_spline_p_mm"] = 1e9
        wp["sigma_spline_R_rad"] = 1e9

    if args.rigid_only:
        tiny = 1e-6
        wp["sigma_delta_mm"] = {j: tiny for j in range(len(joint_names))}
        wp["sigma_deltadot_mm_per_frame"] = {j: tiny for j in range(len(joint_names))}

    solver_opts = {
        "max_num_iterations": int(args.max_iter),
        "num_threads": int(args.threads),
        "verbose": bool(args.verbose),
        "optimize_cameras": bool(args.optimize_cameras),
        "optimize_intrinsics": bool(args.optimize_intrinsics),
    }

    out = mouse_ba.solve(
        cam_quat, cam_trans, cam_intr,
        template_pts,
        obs_cam, obs_mouse, obs_joint, obs_frame,
        obs_x, obs_y, obs_l,

        init_q, init_t,

        joint_names=joint_names,

        mouse_quat=np.asarray(out["mouse_quat"]),
        mouse_trans=np.asarray(out["mouse_trans"]),
        slack=np.asarray(out["slack"]),
        fps=float(args.fps),
        behavior_default=0,
    )

    out_path = Path(args.out)
    out_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    est_df.to_csv(out_path, index=False)
    print(f"Wrote estimated 3D coordinates to: {out_path}")

    if args.gt is not None:
        stats = compare_to_ground_truth(est_df, args.gt)
        print("\\n=== Accuracy vs ground truth (mm) ===")
        print(stats["overall"].to_string(index=False))
        print("\\nPer-mouse:")
        print(stats["per_mouse"].to_string(index=False))
        print("\\nPer-node (worst first):")

        gt_df = pd.read_csv(args.gt)
        print(f"\\nMatched rows: {len(stats['merged'])} (est={len(est_df)}, gt={len(gt_df)})")

if __name__ == "__main__":

Assistant: Here’s the new CLI program you asked for:

[Download baWithPathModel.py](sandbox:/mnt/data/baWithPathModel.py)

It replaces the hard-coded paths in your current `example_run.py` fileciteturn8file0 with CLI arguments, adds an FPS argument (default 10), writes an **estimated** `coords_3d.csv`-style output, and—if you pass a ground-truth `coords_3d.csv`—prints accuracy stats (RMSE/MAE/median/p95/p99, per mouse, per node). ## Built-in ablation switches (already included)
Since you mentioned you’ll likely need an ablation study, I added two flags that don’t require backend changes:

- **Disable path constraint (spline priors):**
```bash
python baWithPathModel.py ... --disable-path
```

- **Rigid-only (force slack offsets ~0):**
```bash
python baWithPathModel.py ... --rigid-only
```

This should help isolate whether non-convergence is driven by (a) path model, (b) slack model, or (c) observation terms.

---

## Why Ceres ends with `NO_CONVERGENCE` in your run
From your log, the solver ran iterations `0..40` and then stopped with `NO_CONVERGENCE`. That typically means **it hit the iteration limit**, not that it diverged. In your earlier `example_run.py`, `max_num_iterations` was set to 40. fileciteturn8file0

The new script defaults to `--max-iter 200`, and you can increase further:
```bash
python baWithPathModel.py ... --max-iter 500
```

Other common causes of “keeps improving but doesn’t converge fast” in *this specific model*:

1) **Rotation spline control points are poorly initialized**  
   In the C++ backend, `ctrl_phi` starts at zero (identity rotation spline) while your per-frame quaternions start from triangulation. This creates a large initial rotation spline residual and can slow convergence significantly.  
   Best fix: initialize `ctrl_phi` from the initial quaternions at knot locations (quat → angle-axis), so the spline starts near the current trajectory.

2) **Robust loss + poor initialization can saturate gradients**  
   If residuals are large initially, Huber/Cauchy will downweight them, making the solver progress slowly. Quick diagnostic: run once with `robust_loss="none"` (or increase Huber delta) and see whether convergence accelerates.

3) **Regularization balance** (path vs slack vs reprojection)  
   If spline priors are too strong, they can “fight” the reprojection residuals; if too weak, occluded periods drift and the optimizer explores too much. The `--disable-path` switch is a good test.

4) **Slack offsets absorbing too much**  
   If slack priors are too loose, the solver can fit 2D observations via slack rather than moving pose, which can make pose and spline variables weakly constrained and slow.

The ground-truth comparison (`--gt`) is the fastest way to tell whether “NO_CONVERGENCE” is actually a problem: you might already have decent accuracy even without meeting strict termination tolerances.

---

If you run `baWithPathModel.py` with `--gt` and paste the printed RMSE tables (overall + per-node), I can tell you very quickly whether the issue is mainly **pose**, **slack**, or **path**, and what weight/initialization change will most likely fix it.

Assistant: ### Why `chmod +x some_script.py` is (usually) **not** necessary
It’s **not** related to Ceres or C/C++ at all.

- If you run a script like this, **no executable bit is needed**:
  ```bash
  python baWithPathModel.py --help
  ```
- The executable bit is only needed if you want to run it *directly* like a program:
  ```bash
  ./baWithPathModel.py --help
  ```
  That relies on the **shebang** line at the top (e.g. `#!/usr/bin/env python3`) to tell Linux which interpreter to use.

So: executable permissions are just a Linux convenience feature; they don’t affect whether Python can load the compiled `mouse_ba*.so` module.

---

## Conventions in `mouse_sim2.py` vs our bundle adjustment assumptions

I went through your simulator code and the key conventions match what we’ve been assuming for BA.

### 1) World coordinate system and units
- Cage origin is at `(0,0,0)` and cage dimensions are `(width=x, depth=y, height=z)`. fileciteturn10file7
- The mice move in the **x–y plane** with `z=0` as ground. Each mouse translation is `Pm = [x, y, 0]`. fileciteturn10file2
- Mouse yaw is a rotation about **world +z** using `rotz(theta)`. fileciteturn10file2

This is consistent with your `cameras.json` scene using the same cage dimensions and origin. fileciteturn10file11

### 2) Rigid template convention (local mouse coordinates)
- Simulator generates *local* mouse keypoints, then transforms to world as:
  \[
  P_w = P_m + R_z(\theta)\,p_{local}
  \]
  exactly as in code. fileciteturn10file2

This matches the BA model style: a rigid template in a body frame transformed by a per-frame pose.

### 3) Camera extrinsics and projection
Your simulator’s camera model is:

- **World → camera** transform:
  \[
  P_c = R\,P_w + t
  \]
  (explicitly implemented). fileciteturn10file3
- Projection:
  \[
  u = f_x \frac{x}{z} + c_x,\quad v = f_y \frac{y}{z} + c_y
  \]
  with the visibility check based on image bounds. fileciteturn10file3
- The `look_at()` builder sets camera axes as **x right, y down, z forward** and uses `t = -R * eye`. fileciteturn10file3

That matches the structure of your exported `cameras.json` (it stores `R`, `t`, and `pos_world`, with `t=-R*pos_world`). fileciteturn10file11  
So: **extrinsic conventions are aligned**.

### 4) 3D output format
Simulator writes:
`frame, time, mouse_id, behavior, node, x, y, z` fileciteturn10file1

That matches your `coords_3d.csv` schema. fileciteturn8file1

And yes: setting `behavior = 0` in BA output is the correct thing to do for your pipeline (behavior gets inferred later). I’ve already done that in `baWithPathModel.py` by writing a constant 0 into that column.

---

## One convention that is “different but OK”
Your simulator sometimes uses behavior labels 0/1/2 (running/rearing/social) in its ground-truth outputs. fileciteturn10file6  
But since you explicitly want BA to output `behavior=0` always (placeholder), that difference is intentional and harmless, as long as the comparison to ground truth ignores that column (my comparison merges only on `frame, mouse_id, node` and compares x/y/z).

---

If you want the strongest possible convention check: the next thing I’d verify is that the **node naming/order** in `dlc_long.csv` matches the template names (`head`, `nose_tip`, etc.) exactly (case/underscore). Your simulator normalizes labels to lowercase with underscores (`_norm_label`). fileciteturn10file6 If DLC output uses a different naming scheme, you’d need a mapping layer in the front-end.

import os, stat, textwrap

code = """#!/usr/bin/env python3
\"\"\"
baWithPathModel.py

CLI wrapper around the Ceres backend (mouse_ba) using a Python front-end.

- Reads cameras.json, mouse template (.txt), and dlc_long.csv
- Initializes per-frame mouse poses from multi-view triangulation
- Runs model-based BA with soft spline (path) priors + rigid template + tiny slack offsets
- Writes estimated 3D body-part coordinates in coords_3d.csv format
- Optionally compares against ground-truth coords_3d.csv and prints accuracy stats

Important convention:
- The ordering / naming of joints is taken from frontend.JOINTS, and template points are read
  via frontend.load_template_points(). This guarantees consistency between:
  (a) how DLC observations are mapped to joint indices, and
  (b) the template point ordering passed into the Ceres backend.
\"\"\"

from __future__ import annotations

import argparse
import sys
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict

import numpy as np
import pandas as pd


def _auto_add_build_to_syspath() -> None:
    \"\"\"Make 'import mouse_ba' work without requiring PYTHONPATH.\"\"\"
    script_dir = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
    build_dir = script_dir.parent / \"build\"
    if build_dir.exists():
        sys.path.insert(0, str(build_dir))


_auto_add_build_to_syspath()

# Local front-end helpers
from frontend import (
    JOINTS,
    load_cameras_json,
    load_template_points,
    load_dlc_long_csv,
    init_poses_from_triangulation,
    default_weight_pack,
)

import mouse_ba


# -----------------------------
# Quaternion helpers (w,x,y,z)
# -----------------------------
def quat_normalize(q: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
    n = np.linalg.norm(q, axis=-1, keepdims=True)
    n = np.where(n == 0.0, 1.0, n)
    return q / n


def quat_to_rotmat_wxyz(q: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
    \"\"\"q: (...,4) in (w,x,y,z). returns (...,3,3).\"\"\"
    q = quat_normalize(q)
    w, x, y, z = q[..., 0], q[..., 1], q[..., 2], q[..., 3]
    ww, xx, yy, zz = w*w, x*x, y*y, z*z
    wx, wy, wz = w*x, w*y, w*z
    xy, xz, yz = x*y, x*z, y*z

    R = np.empty(q.shape[:-1] + (3, 3), dtype=np.float64)
    R[..., 0, 0] = ww + xx - yy - zz
    R[..., 0, 1] = 2.0 * (xy - wz)
    R[..., 0, 2] = 2.0 * (xz + wy)

    R[..., 1, 0] = 2.0 * (xy + wz)
    R[..., 1, 1] = ww - xx + yy - zz
    R[..., 1, 2] = 2.0 * (yz - wx)

    R[..., 2, 0] = 2.0 * (xz - wy)
    R[..., 2, 1] = 2.0 * (yz + wx)
    R[..., 2, 2] = ww - xx - yy + zz
    return R


# -----------------------------
# Estimation -> coords_3d.csv
# -----------------------------
def build_estimated_coords_df(
    template_pts: np.ndarray,           # (J,3) ordered like JOINTS
    mouse_quat: np.ndarray,             # (M,T,4) wxyz
    mouse_trans: np.ndarray,            # (M,T,3)
    slack: np.ndarray,                  # (M,T,J,3)
    fps: float,
    behavior_default: int = 0,
) -> pd.DataFrame:
    \"\"\"Produces DataFrame with columns of coords_3d.csv.\"\"\"
    M, T, J, _ = slack.shape
    assert template_pts.shape == (J, 3)

    R = quat_to_rotmat_wxyz(mouse_quat)   # (M,T,3,3)
    local = template_pts[None, None, :, :] + slack
    world = (R[..., None, :, :] @ local[..., None]).squeeze(-1) + mouse_trans[..., None, :]

    frames = np.arange(T, dtype=np.int32)
    times = frames.astype(np.float64) / float(fps)

    recs = []
    for m in range(M):
        for t in range(T):
            for j in range(J):
                recs.append((
                    int(frames[t]),
                    float(times[t]),
                    int(m),
                    int(behavior_default),
                    JOINTS[j],
                    float(world[m, t, j, 0]),
                    float(world[m, t, j, 1]),
                    float(world[m, t, j, 2]),
                ))
    return pd.DataFrame(recs, columns=[\"frame\", \"time\", \"mouse_id\", \"behavior\", \"node\", \"x\", \"y\", \"z\"])


def compare_to_ground_truth(est_df: pd.DataFrame, gt_path: str | Path) -> Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]:
    \"\"\"Compare estimates to coords_3d.csv ground truth; returns summary tables.\"\"\"
    gt_df = pd.read_csv(gt_path)
    required = {\"frame\", \"mouse_id\", \"node\", \"x\", \"y\", \"z\"}
    missing = required - set(gt_df.columns)
    if missing:
        raise ValueError(f\"Ground truth file missing required columns: {sorted(missing)}\")

    keys = [\"frame\", \"mouse_id\", \"node\"]
    m = est_df.merge(gt_df[keys + [\"x\", \"y\", \"z\"]], on=keys, suffixes=(\"_est\", \"_gt\"), how=\"inner\")
    if len(m) == 0:
        raise ValueError(\"No matching rows between estimate and ground truth (check node names / frame count).\")

    dx = m[\"x_est\"].to_numpy() - m[\"x_gt\"].to_numpy()
    dy = m[\"y_est\"].to_numpy() - m[\"y_gt\"].to_numpy()
    dz = m[\"z_est\"].to_numpy() - m[\"z_gt\"].to_numpy()
    err = np.sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy + dz*dz)
    m[\"err_mm\"] = err

    overall = pd.DataFrame([{
        \"N\": int(len(err)),
        \"RMSE_mm\": float(np.sqrt(np.mean(err**2))),
        \"MAE_mm\": float(np.mean(np.abs(err))),
        \"Median_mm\": float(np.median(err)),
        \"P95_mm\": float(np.percentile(err, 95)),
        \"P99_mm\": float(np.percentile(err, 99)),
    }])

    per_node = (
        m.groupby(\"node\")[\"err_mm\"]
         .agg(
             N=\"count\",
             RMSE_mm=lambda x: float(np.sqrt(np.mean(np.square(x)))),
             MAE_mm=\"mean\",
             Median_mm=\"median\",
             P95_mm=lambda x: float(np.percentile(x, 95)),
         )
         .reset_index()
         .sort_values(\"RMSE_mm\", ascending=False)
    )

    per_mouse = (
        m.groupby(\"mouse_id\")[\"err_mm\"]
         .agg(
             N=\"count\",
             RMSE_mm=lambda x: float(np.sqrt(np.mean(np.square(x)))),
             MAE_mm=\"mean\",
             Median_mm=\"median\",
             P95_mm=lambda x: float(np.percentile(x, 95)),
         )
         .reset_index()
         .sort_values(\"mouse_id\")
    )

    return {\"overall\": overall, \"per_node\": per_node, \"per_mouse\": per_mouse, \"merged\": m}


# -----------------------------
# CLI + main
# -----------------------------
def build_arg_parser() -> argparse.ArgumentParser:
    p = argparse.ArgumentParser(
        prog=\"baWithPathModel.py\",
        description=\"Model-based BA with soft spline priors + rigid template + tiny slack offsets.\",
    )
    p.add_argument(\"--cameras\", required=True, help=\"Path to cameras.json\")
    p.add_argument(\"--template\", required=True, help=\"Path to mouse template file (e.g., mouse3_mesh_shortTail.txt)\")
    p.add_argument(\"--dlc\", required=True, help=\"Path to DLC long-format CSV (dlc_long.csv)\")
    p.add_argument(\"--fps\", type=float, default=10.0, help=\"Frames per second (default: 10)\")
    p.add_argument(\"--out\", required=True, help=\"Output CSV path for estimated 3D coordinates (coords_3d.csv format)\")
    p.add_argument(\"--gt\", default=None, help=\"Optional ground-truth coords_3d.csv to compare against\")

    p.add_argument(\"--init-likelihood-min\", type=float, default=0.2,
                   help=\"Likelihood threshold for triangulation-based initialization (default: 0.2)\")

    p.add_argument(\"--max-iter\", type=int, default=200, help=\"Ceres max iterations (default: 200)\")
    p.add_argument(\"--threads\", type=int, default=8, help=\"Ceres threads (default: 8)\")
    p.add_argument(\"--verbose\", action=\"store_true\", help=\"Print Ceres iteration table\")
    p.add_argument(\"--optimize-cameras\", action=\"store_true\", help=\"Estimate camera extrinsics (default off)\")
    p.add_argument(\"--optimize-intrinsics\", action=\"store_true\", help=\"Estimate camera intrinsics (default off)\")

    # Ablation switches
    p.add_argument(\"--disable-path\", action=\"store_true\",
                   help=\"Disable spline/path priors by setting their weights ~0.\")
    p.add_argument(\"--rigid-only\", action=\"store_true\",
                   help=\"Force slack offsets ~0 (pure rigid template).\")
    return p


def main() -> int:
    args = build_arg_parser().parse_args()

    cam_quat, cam_trans, cam_intr = load_cameras_json(args.cameras)
    template_pts = load_template_points(args.template)

    (obs_cam, obs_mouse, obs_joint, obs_frame,
     obs_x, obs_y, obs_l, num_frames) = load_dlc_long_csv(args.dlc)

    init_q, init_t = init_poses_from_triangulation(
        template_pts,
        obs_cam, obs_mouse, obs_joint, obs_frame, obs_x, obs_y, obs_l,
        cam_quat, cam_trans, cam_intr,
        likelihood_min=args.init_likelihood_min,
    )

    wp = default_weight_pack().to_dict()

    # knot interval ≈ 0.3s worth of frames, min 3
    wp[\"knot_interval_frames\"] = max(3, int(round(args.fps * 0.3)))

    if args.disable_path:
        wp[\"sigma_spline_p_mm\"] = 1e9
        wp[\"sigma_spline_R_rad\"] = 1e9

    if args.rigid_only:
        tiny = 1e-6
        wp[\"sigma_delta_mm\"] = {j: tiny for j in range(len(JOINTS))}
        wp[\"sigma_deltadot_mm_per_frame\"] = {j: tiny for j in range(len(JOINTS))}

    solver_opts = {
        \"max_num_iterations\": int(args.max_iter),
        \"num_threads\": int(args.threads),
        \"verbose\": bool(args.verbose),
        \"optimize_cameras\": bool(args.optimize_cameras),
        \"optimize_intrinsics\": bool(args.optimize_intrinsics),
    }

    out = mouse_ba.solve(
        cam_quat, cam_trans, cam_intr,
        template_pts,
        obs_cam, obs_mouse, obs_joint, obs_frame,
        obs_x, obs_y, obs_l,
        int(num_frames),
        init_q, init_t,
        wp,
        solver_opts,
    )

    print(out[\"summary\"])

    est_df = build_estimated_coords_df(
        template_pts=template_pts,
        mouse_quat=np.asarray(out[\"mouse_quat\"]),
        mouse_trans=np.asarray(out[\"mouse_trans\"]),
        slack=np.asarray(out[\"slack\"]),
        fps=float(args.fps),
        behavior_default=0,
    )

    out_path = Path(args.out)
    out_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    est_df.to_csv(out_path, index=False)
    print(f\"Wrote estimated 3D coordinates to: {out_path}\")

    if args.gt is not None:
        stats = compare_to_ground_truth(est_df, args.gt)
        print(\"\\n=== Accuracy vs ground truth (mm) ===\")
        print(stats[\"overall\"].to_string(index=False))
        print(\"\\nPer-mouse:\")
        print(stats[\"per_mouse\"].to_string(index=False))
        print(\"\\nPer-node (worst first):\")
        print(stats[\"per_node\"].to_string(index=False))

        gt_df = pd.read_csv(args.gt)
        print(f\"\\nMatched rows: {len(stats['merged'])} (est={len(est_df)}, gt={len(gt_df)})\")

    return 0


if __name__ == \"__main__\":
    raise SystemExit(main())

code = """#!/usr/bin/env python3

from __future__ import annotations

import argparse
import sys
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict

import numpy as np

from frontend import (
    JOINTS,
    load_cameras_json,
    load_template_points,
    load_dlc_long_csv,
    init_poses_from_triangulation,
    default_weight_pack,
)

import mouse_ba


def quat_normalize(q: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
    n = np.linalg.norm(q, axis=-1, keepdims=True)
    n = np.where(n == 0.0, 1.0, n)
    return q / n


def quat_to_rotmat_wxyz(q: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
    q = quat_normalize(q)
    w, x, y, z = q[..., 0], q[..., 1], q[..., 2], q[..., 3]
    ww, xx, yy, zz = w*w, x*x, y*y, z*z
    wx, wy, wz = w*x, w*y, w*z
    xy, xz, yz = x*y, x*z, y*z

    R = np.empty(q.shape[:-1] + (3, 3), dtype=np.float64)
    R[..., 0, 0] = ww + xx - yy - zz
    R[..., 0, 1] = 2.0 * (xy - wz)
    R[..., 0, 2] = 2.0 * (xz + wy)

    R[..., 1, 0] = 2.0 * (xy + wz)
    R[..., 1, 1] = ww - xx + yy - zz
    R[..., 1, 2] = 2.0 * (yz - wx)

    R[..., 2, 0] = 2.0 * (xz - wy)
    R[..., 2, 1] = 2.0 * (yz + wx)
    R[..., 2, 2] = ww - xx - yy + zz
    return R


def build_estimated_coords_df(
    template_pts: np.ndarray,
    mouse_quat: np.ndarray,
    mouse_trans: np.ndarray,
    slack: np.ndarray,
    fps: float,
    behavior_default: int = 0,
) -> pd.DataFrame:
    M, T, J, _ = slack.shape
    assert template_pts.shape == (J, 3)

    R = quat_to_rotmat_wxyz(mouse_quat)
    local = template_pts[None, None, :, :] + slack
    world = (R[..., None, :, :] @ local[..., None]).squeeze(-1) + mouse_trans[..., None, :]

    frames = np.arange(T, dtype=np.int32)
    times = frames.astype(np.float64) / float(fps)

    recs = []
    for m in range(M):
        for t in range(T):
            for j in range(J):
                recs.append((
                    int(frames[t]),
                    float(times[t]),
                    int(m),
                    int(behavior_default),
                    JOINTS[j],
                    float(world[m, t, j, 0]),
                    float(world[m, t, j, 1]),
                    float(world[m, t, j, 2]),
                ))
    return pd.DataFrame(recs, columns=["frame", "time", "mouse_id", "behavior", "node", "x", "y", "z"])


def compare_to_ground_truth(est_df: pd.DataFrame, gt_path: str | Path) -> Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]:
    gt_df = pd.read_csv(gt_path)
    required = {"frame", "mouse_id", "node", "x", "y", "z"}
    missing = required - set(gt_df.columns)
    if missing:
        raise ValueError(f"Ground truth file missing required columns: {sorted(missing)}")

    keys = ["frame", "mouse_id", "node"]
    m = est_df.merge(gt_df[keys + ["x", "y", "z"]], on=keys, suffixes=("_est", "_gt"), how="inner")
    if len(m) == 0:
        raise ValueError("No matching rows between estimate and ground truth (check node names / frame count).")

    dx = m["x_est"].to_numpy() - m["x_gt"].to_numpy()
    dy = m["y_est"].to_numpy() - m["y_gt"].to_numpy()
    dz = m["z_est"].to_numpy() - m["z_gt"].to_numpy()
    err = np.sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy + dz*dz)
    m["err_mm"] = err

    overall = pd.DataFrame([{
        "N": int(len(err)),
        "RMSE_mm": float(np.sqrt(np.mean(err**2))),
        "MAE_mm": float(np.mean(np.abs(err))),
        "Median_mm": float(np.median(err)),
        "P95_mm": float(np.percentile(err, 95)),
        "P99_mm": float(np.percentile(err, 99)),
    }])

    per_node = (
        m.groupby("node")["err_mm"]
         .agg(
             N="count",
             RMSE_mm=lambda x: float(np.sqrt(np.mean(np.square(x)))),
             MAE_mm="mean",
             Median_mm="median",
             P95_mm=lambda x: float(np.percentile(x, 95)),
         )
         .reset_index()
         .sort_values("RMSE_mm", ascending=False)
    )

    per_mouse = (
        m.groupby("mouse_id")["err_mm"]
         .agg(
             N="count",
             RMSE_mm=lambda x: float(np.sqrt(np.mean(np.square(x)))),
             MAE_mm="mean",
             Median_mm="median",
             P95_mm=lambda x: float(np.percentile(x, 95)),
         )
         .reset_index()
         .sort_values("mouse_id")
    )

    return {"overall": overall, "per_node": per_node, "per_mouse": per_mouse, "merged": m}


def build_arg_parser() -> argparse.ArgumentParser:
    p = argparse.ArgumentParser(
        prog="baWithPathModel_v2.py",
        description="Model-based BA with soft spline priors + rigid template + tiny slack offsets.",
    )
    p.add_argument("--cameras", required=True, help="Path to cameras.json")
    p.add_argument("--template", required=True, help="Path to mouse template file (mouse3_mesh_shortTail.txt)")
    p.add_argument("--dlc", required=True, help="Path to DLC long-format CSV (dlc_long.csv)")
    p.add_argument("--fps", type=float, default=10.0, help="Frames per second (default: 10)")
    p.add_argument("--out", required=True, help="Output CSV path for estimated 3D coordinates (coords_3d.csv format)")
    p.add_argument("--gt", default=None, help="Optional ground-truth coords_3d.csv to compare against")

    p.add_argument("--init-likelihood-min", type=float, default=0.2,
                   help="Likelihood threshold for triangulation-based initialization (default: 0.2)")

    p.add_argument("--max-iter", type=int, default=200, help="Ceres max iterations (default: 200)")
    p.add_argument("--threads", type=int, default=8, help="Ceres threads (default: 8)")
    p.add_argument("--verbose", action="store_true", help="Print Ceres iteration table")
    p.add_argument("--optimize-cameras", action="store_true", help="Estimate camera extrinsics (default off)")
    p.add_argument("--optimize-intrinsics", action="store_true", help="Estimate camera intrinsics (default off)")

    p.add_argument("--disable-path", action="store_true",
                   help="Disable spline/path priors by setting their weights ~0.")
    p.add_argument("--rigid-only", action="store_true",
                   help="Force slack offsets ~0 (pure rigid template).")
    return p


def main() -> int:
    args = build_arg_parser().parse_args()

    cam_quat, cam_trans, cam_intr = load_cameras_json(args.cameras)
    template_pts = load_template_points(args.template)

    (obs_cam, obs_mouse, obs_joint, obs_frame,
     obs_x, obs_y, obs_l, num_frames) = load_dlc_long_csv(args.dlc)

    init_q, init_t = init_poses_from_triangulation(
        template_pts,
        obs_cam, obs_mouse, obs_joint, obs_frame, obs_x, obs_y, obs_l,
        cam_quat, cam_trans, cam_intr,
        likelihood_min=args.init_likelihood_min,
    )

    wp = default_weight_pack().to_dict()
    wp["knot_interval_frames"] = max(3, int(round(args.fps * 0.3)))

    if args.disable_path:
        wp["sigma_spline_p_mm"] = 1e9
        wp["sigma_spline_R_rad"] = 1e9

    if args.rigid_only:
        tiny = 1e-6
        wp["sigma_delta_mm"] = {j: tiny for j in range(len(JOINTS))}
        wp["sigma_deltadot_mm_per_frame"] = {j: tiny for j in range(len(JOINTS))}

    solver_opts = {
        "max_num_iterations": int(args.max_iter),
        "num_threads": int(args.threads),
        "verbose": bool(args.verbose),
        "optimize_cameras": bool(args.optimize_cameras),
        "optimize_intrinsics": bool(args.optimize_intrinsics),
    }

    out = mouse_ba.solve(
        cam_quat, cam_trans, cam_intr,
        template_pts,
        obs_cam, obs_mouse, obs_joint, obs_frame,
        obs_x, obs_y, obs_l,
        int(num_frames),
        init_q, init_t,
        wp,
        solver_opts,
    )

    print(out["summary"])

    est_df = build_estimated_coords_df(
        template_pts=template_pts,
        mouse_quat=np.asarray(out["mouse_quat"]),
        mouse_trans=np.asarray(out["mouse_trans"]),
        slack=np.asarray(out["slack"]),
        fps=float(args.fps),
        behavior_default=0,
    )

    out_path = Path(args.out)
    out_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    est_df.to_csv(out_path, index=False)
    print(f"Wrote estimated 3D coordinates to: {out_path}")

    if args.gt is not None:
        stats = compare_to_ground_truth(est_df, args.gt)
        print("\\n=== Accuracy vs ground truth (mm) ===")
        print(stats["overall"].to_string(index=False))
        print("\\nPer-mouse:")
        print(stats["per_mouse"].to_string(index=False))
        print("\\nPer-node (worst first):")
        print(stats["per_node"].to_string(index=False))

        gt_df = pd.read_csv(args.gt)
        print(f"\\nMatched rows: {len(stats['merged'])} (est={len(est_df)}, gt={len(gt_df)})")

    return 0


if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main())

Assistant: You didn’t make a mistake.

`baWithPathModel.py` failed because **its template parser was too strict**: it expected the template file to start immediately with lines like:

```
name x y z
```

…but your template file actually begins with a section header:

```
[NODES]
head ...
...
[EDGES]
...
```

That’s exactly why `example_run.py` worked: it uses `frontend.load_template_points(...)`, which already understands the `[NODES]` format and (crucially) returns points in the **same joint order** that the DLC loader uses. In contrast, my first `baWithPathModel.py` tried to infer joint order from the file itself, which is not what your pipeline assumes.

### Fixed script
Use this corrected version that reuses `frontend.load_template_points()` and `frontend.JOINTS` (so conventions match `example_run.py`):

[Download baWithPathModel_v2.py](sandbox:/mnt/data/baWithPathModel_v2.py)

### How to run (same as before, just the filename)
```bash
python baWithPathModel_v2.py \
  --cameras ../cameras.json \
  --template ../mouse3_mesh_shortTail.txt \
  --dlc ../dlc_long.csv \
  --fps 10 \
  --out ../coords_3d_est.csv \
  --gt ../../mouse_sim/out2m_2/coords_3d.csv \
  --verbose
```

It always writes `behavior = 0` in the output (as you want), and the GT comparison ignores the behavior column.

---

## Why this matters beyond the error
Even if my old parser had been fixed to read `[NODES]`, it still would’ve been risky because **joint ordering must match the indices used in the DLC long CSV mapping**. `frontend.JOINTS` defines the canonical order, and `frontend.load_template_points()` fills template points into that order. That’s the safe/consistent choice.

Assistant: from pathlib import Path
import os, stat, textwrap

code = r"""#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
code += r'''
"""baWithPathModel_v3.py

Model-based bundle adjustment (Ceres backend) with:
- rigid mouse template
- tiny slack offsets
- soft spline path priors

Adds:
- CLI to select input files + FPS
- writes estimated coords_3d.csv
- optional GT comparison with diagnostics:
    * auto-detect quaternion coefficient order (wxyz vs xyzw) when --quat-order=auto
    * optional global mouse-id swap test
- optional video rendering (three cameras) similar to mouse_sim2.py

Run:
  python baWithPathModel_v3.py --help
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import argparse
import sys
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, Tuple, Optional, List

import numpy as np
import pandas as pd

# Optional video backend (same policy as mouse_sim2.py)
_VIDEO_BACKEND = None
try:
    import cv2  # type: ignore
    _VIDEO_BACKEND = "opencv"
except Exception:
    cv2 = None  # type: ignore

if _VIDEO_BACKEND is None:
    try:
        import imageio.v2 as imageio  # type: ignore
        _VIDEO_BACKEND = "imageio"
    except Exception:
        imageio = None  # type: ignore


def _auto_add_build_to_syspath() -> None:
    """Make 'import mouse_ba' work without requiring PYTHONPATH."""
    script_dir = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
    build_dir = script_dir.parent / "build"
    if build_dir.exists():
        sys.path.insert(0, str(build_dir))


_auto_add_build_to_syspath()

from frontend import (
    JOINTS,
    load_cameras_json,
    load_template_points,
    load_dlc_long_csv,
    init_poses_from_triangulation,
    default_weight_pack,
)

import mouse_ba


# -----------------------------
# Quaternion helpers
# -----------------------------
def quat_normalize(q: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
    n = np.linalg.norm(q, axis=-1, keepdims=True)
    n = np.where(n == 0.0, 1.0, n)
    return q / n


def quat_to_rotmat(q: np.ndarray, order: str) -> np.ndarray:
    """
    Convert quaternion array to rotation matrices.
    order:
      - "wxyz": q = (w, x, y, z)
      - "xyzw": q = (x, y, z, w)  (Eigen coefficient order)
    """
    q = quat_normalize(q)
    if order == "wxyz":
        w, x, y, z = q[..., 0], q[..., 1], q[..., 2], q[..., 3]
    elif order == "xyzw":
        x, y, z, w = q[..., 0], q[..., 1], q[..., 2], q[..., 3]
    else:
        raise ValueError(f"Unknown quaternion order: {order}")

    ww, xx, yy, zz = w*w, x*x, y*y, z*z
    wx, wy, wz = w*x, w*y, w*z
    xy, xz, yz = x*y, x*z, y*z

    R = np.empty(q.shape[:-1] + (3, 3), dtype=np.float64)
    R[..., 0, 0] = ww + xx - yy - zz
    R[..., 0, 1] = 2.0 * (xy - wz)
    R[..., 0, 2] = 2.0 * (xz + wy)

    R[..., 1, 0] = 2.0 * (xy + wz)
    R[..., 1, 1] = ww - xx + yy - zz
    R[..., 1, 2] = 2.0 * (yz - wx)

    R[..., 2, 0] = 2.0 * (xz - wy)
    R[..., 2, 1] = 2.0 * (yz + wx)
    R[..., 2, 2] = ww - xx - yy + zz
    return R


# -----------------------------
# coords_3d.csv writer + GT comparison
# -----------------------------
def build_estimated_coords_df(
    template_pts: np.ndarray,           # (J,3) ordered like JOINTS
    mouse_quat: np.ndarray,             # (M,T,4)
    mouse_trans: np.ndarray,            # (M,T,3)
    slack: np.ndarray,                  # (M,T,J,3)
    fps: float,
    quat_order: str,
    behavior_default: int = 0,
    mouse_id_swap: bool = False,
) -> pd.DataFrame:
    """Produces DataFrame with coords_3d.csv columns."""
    M, T, J, _ = slack.shape
    assert template_pts.shape == (J, 3)
    assert mouse_quat.shape[:2] == (M, T)
    assert mouse_trans.shape[:2] == (M, T)

    R = quat_to_rotmat(mouse_quat, quat_order)   # (M,T,3,3)
    local = template_pts[None, None, :, :] + slack
    world = (R[..., None, :, :] @ local[..., None]).squeeze(-1) + mouse_trans[..., None, :]

    frames = np.arange(T, dtype=np.int32)
    times = frames.astype(np.float64) / float(fps)

    # optional global swap for diagnostics
    if mouse_id_swap and M == 2:
        world = world[[1, 0], ...]  # swap mice

    recs = []
    for m in range(M):
        for t in range(T):
            for j in range(J):
                recs.append((
                    int(frames[t]),
                    float(times[t]),
                    int(m),
                    int(behavior_default),
                    JOINTS[j],
                    float(world[m, t, j, 0]),
                    float(world[m, t, j, 1]),
                    float(world[m, t, j, 2]),
                ))
    return pd.DataFrame(recs, columns=["frame", "time", "mouse_id", "behavior", "node", "x", "y", "z"])


def compare_to_ground_truth(est_df: pd.DataFrame, gt_path: str | Path) -> Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]:
    """Compare estimates to coords_3d.csv ground truth; returns summary tables."""
    gt_df = pd.read_csv(gt_path)
    required = {"frame", "mouse_id", "node", "x", "y", "z"}
    missing = required - set(gt_df.columns)
    if missing:
        raise ValueError(f"Ground truth file missing required columns: {sorted(missing)}")

    keys = ["frame", "mouse_id", "node"]
    m = est_df.merge(gt_df[keys + ["x", "y", "z"]], on=keys, suffixes=("_est", "_gt"), how="inner")
    if len(m) == 0:
        raise ValueError("No matching rows between estimate and ground truth (check node names / frame count).")

    dx = m["x_est"].to_numpy() - m["x_gt"].to_numpy()
    dy = m["y_est"].to_numpy() - m["y_gt"].to_numpy()
    dz = m["z_est"].to_numpy() - m["z_gt"].to_numpy()
    err = np.sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy + dz*dz)
    m["err_mm"] = err

    overall = pd.DataFrame([{
        "N": int(len(err)),
        "RMSE_mm": float(np.sqrt(np.mean(err**2))),
        "MAE_mm": float(np.mean(np.abs(err))),
        "Median_mm": float(np.median(err)),
        "P95_mm": float(np.percentile(err, 95)),
        "P99_mm": float(np.percentile(err, 99)),
    }])

    per_node = (
        m.groupby("node")["err_mm"]
         .agg(
             N="count",
             RMSE_mm=lambda x: float(np.sqrt(np.mean(np.square(x)))),
             MAE_mm="mean",
             Median_mm="median",
             P95_mm=lambda x: float(np.percentile(x, 95)),
         )
         .reset_index()
         .sort_values("RMSE_mm", ascending=False)
    )

    per_mouse = (
        m.groupby("mouse_id")["err_mm"]
         .agg(
             N="count",
             RMSE_mm=lambda x: float(np.sqrt(np.mean(np.square(x)))),
             MAE_mm="mean",
             Median_mm="median",
             P95_mm=lambda x: float(np.percentile(x, 95)),
         )
         .reset_index()
         .sort_values("mouse_id")
    )

    # quick offset diagnostics (mean vector, per axis)
    offs = pd.DataFrame([{
        "mean_dx": float(dx.mean()),
        "mean_dy": float(dy.mean()),
        "mean_dz": float(dz.mean()),
        "std_dx": float(dx.std()),
        "std_dy": float(dy.std()),
        "std_dz": float(dz.std()),
    }])

    return {"overall": overall, "per_node": per_node, "per_mouse": per_mouse, "offsets": offs, "merged": m}


# -----------------------------
# Video rendering (optional)
# -----------------------------
class Camera:
    def __init__(self, name: str, width: int, height: int, fx: float, fy: float, cx: float, cy: float,
                 R: np.ndarray, t: np.ndarray):
        self.name = name
        self.width = int(width)
        self.height = int(height)
        self.fx = float(fx)
        self.fy = float(fy)
        self.cx = float(cx)
        self.cy = float(cy)
        self.R = np.asarray(R, dtype=np.float64).reshape(3, 3)
        self.t = np.asarray(t, dtype=np.float64).reshape(3,)

    def project(self, Pw: np.ndarray) -> Tuple[float, float, bool]:
        Pc = self.R @ Pw + self.t
        z = Pc[2]
        if z <= 1e-6:
            return 0.0, 0.0, False
        u = self.fx * (Pc[0] / z) + self.cx
        v = self.fy * (Pc[1] / z) + self.cy
        vis = (0.0 <= u < self.width) and (0.0 <= v < self.height)
        return float(u), float(v), bool(vis)


def parse_edges_from_template(path: str | Path) -> List[Tuple[str, str]]:
    """Parse [EDGES] section from template file."""
    p = Path(path)
    edges: List[Tuple[str, str]] = []
    in_edges = False
    for line in p.read_text(encoding="utf-8").splitlines():
        s = line.strip()
        if not s:
            continue
        if s.upper() == "[EDGES]":
            in_edges = True
            continue
        if s.startswith("[") and s.endswith("]") and s.upper() != "[EDGES]":
            in_edges = False
        if in_edges:
            parts = s.split()
            if len(parts) == 2:
                edges.append((parts[0], parts[1]))
    return edges


def render_frame_two(
    cam: Camera,
    edges: List[Tuple[str, str]],
    world_nodes_by_mouse: List[Dict[str, np.ndarray]],
    cage_w: float, cage_d: float, cage_h: float,
    draw_labels: bool = False,
) -> np.ndarray:
    """Render one frame like mouse_sim2.py (black background, cage + skeletons)."""
    img = np.zeros((cam.height, cam.width, 3), dtype=np.uint8)
    if cv2 is None:
        return img

    # cage corners
    cage_pts = []
    for x in (0.0, cage_w):
        for y in (0.0, cage_d):
            for z in (0.0, cage_h):
                cage_pts.append(np.array([x, y, z], dtype=np.float64))
    cage_pts = np.array(cage_pts)

    corner_index = {(x, y, z): i for i, (x, y, z) in enumerate(
        [(x, y, z) for x in (0.0, cage_w) for y in (0.0, cage_d) for z in (0.0, cage_h)]
    )}
    def idx(x, y, z): return corner_index[(x, y, z)]
    box_edges = [
        (idx(0.0, 0.0, 0.0), idx(cage_w, 0.0, 0.0)),
        (idx(0.0, 0.0, 0.0), idx(0.0, cage_d, 0.0)),
        (idx(cage_w, 0.0, 0.0), idx(cage_w, cage_d, 0.0)),
        (idx(0.0, cage_d, 0.0), idx(cage_w, cage_d, 0.0)),
        (idx(0.0, 0.0, cage_h), idx(cage_w, 0.0, cage_h)),
        (idx(0.0, 0.0, cage_h), idx(0.0, cage_d, cage_h)),
        (idx(cage_w, 0.0, cage_h), idx(cage_w, cage_d, cage_h)),
        (idx(0.0, cage_d, cage_h), idx(cage_w, cage_d, cage_h)),
        (idx(0.0, 0.0, 0.0), idx(0.0, 0.0, cage_h)),
        (idx(cage_w, 0.0, 0.0), idx(cage_w, 0.0, cage_h)),
        (idx(0.0, cage_d, 0.0), idx(0.0, cage_d, cage_h)),
        (idx(cage_w, cage_d, 0.0), idx(cage_w, cage_d, cage_h)),
    ]
    cage_uv = []
    for p in cage_pts:
        u, v, vis = cam.project(p)
        cage_uv.append((u, v, vis))
    for a, b in box_edges:
        ua, va, visa = cage_uv[a]
        ub, vb, visb = cage_uv[b]
        if visa and visb:
            cv2.line(img, (int(ua), int(va)), (int(ub), int(vb)), (60, 60, 60), 1, cv2.LINE_AA)

    colors = [(255, 255, 255), (80, 220, 80)]
    node_cols = [(255, 255, 255), (120, 255, 120)]

    for mi, world_nodes in enumerate(world_nodes_by_mouse):
        col = colors[mi % len(colors)]
        coln = node_cols[mi % len(node_cols)]

        # skeleton edges
        for a, b in edges:
            if a not in world_nodes or b not in world_nodes:
                continue
            ua, va, visa = cam.project(world_nodes[a])
            ub, vb, visb = cam.project(world_nodes[b])
            if visa and visb:
                cv2.line(img, (int(ua), int(va)), (int(ub), int(vb)), col, 2, cv2.LINE_AA)

        # nodes
        for label, Pw in world_nodes.items():
            u, v, vis = cam.project(Pw)
            if not vis:
                continue
            cv2.circle(img, (int(u), int(v)), 4, coln, -1, cv2.LINE_AA)
            if draw_labels:
                cv2.putText(img, f"{mi}:{label}", (int(u) + 5, int(v) - 5),
                            cv2.FONT_HERSHEY_SIMPLEX, 0.4, coln, 1, cv2.LINE_AA)

    return img


def write_videos(
    cameras_json_path: str | Path,
    template_path: str | Path,
    coords_df: pd.DataFrame,
    out_dir: str | Path,
    fps: float,
    draw_labels: bool = False,
) -> None:
    """Write one mp4 per camera name, like mouse_sim2.py."""
    if _VIDEO_BACKEND is None:
        raise RuntimeError("No video backend available. Install opencv or imageio.")

    cj = pd.read_json(cameras_json_path)
    # pandas may coerce; load via json
    import json
    scene = json.loads(Path(cameras_json_path).read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    cage = scene["cage"]
    cage_w, cage_d, cage_h = float(cage["width"]), float(cage["depth"]), float(cage["height"])
    cams = []
    for c in scene["cameras"]:
        cams.append(Camera(
            name=c["name"],
            width=c["width"], height=c["height"],
            fx=c["fx"], fy=c["fy"], cx=c["cx"], cy=c["cy"],
            R=np.array(c["R"], dtype=np.float64),
            t=np.array(c["t"], dtype=np.float64),
        ))

    edges = parse_edges_from_template(template_path)

    out_dir = Path(out_dir)
    out_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    # prepare per-frame per-mouse dicts for fast lookup
    # coords_df has rows for all frames/mice/nodes
    frames = sorted(coords_df["frame"].unique())
    mice = sorted(coords_df["mouse_id"].unique())

    # group: (frame, mouse_id) -> dict(node -> Pw)
    grouped: Dict[Tuple[int, int], Dict[str, np.ndarray]] = {}
    for (fr, mid), g in coords_df.groupby(["frame", "mouse_id"]):
        d = {row["node"]: np.array([row["x"], row["y"], row["z"]], dtype=np.float64) for _, row in g.iterrows()}
        grouped[(int(fr), int(mid))] = d

    writers = {}
    if _VIDEO_BACKEND == "opencv":
        fourcc = cv2.VideoWriter_fourcc(*"mp4v")  # type: ignore
        for cam in cams:
            path = str(out_dir / f"{cam.name}.mp4")
            writers[cam.name] = cv2.VideoWriter(path, fourcc, float(fps), (cam.width, cam.height))  # type: ignore
    else:
        for cam in cams:
            path = str(out_dir / f"{cam.name}.mp4")
            writers[cam.name] = imageio.get_writer(path, fps=float(fps))  # type: ignore

    try:
        for fr in frames:
            world_nodes_by_mouse = [grouped.get((int(fr), int(mid)), {}) for mid in mice]
            for cam in cams:
                img = render_frame_two(cam, edges, world_nodes_by_mouse, cage_w, cage_d, cage_h, draw_labels=draw_labels)
                if _VIDEO_BACKEND == "opencv":
                    writers[cam.name].write(img)  # type: ignore
                else:
                    writers[cam.name].append_data(img[..., ::-1])  # BGR->RGB
    finally:
        for w in writers.values():
            try:
                w.release()  # type: ignore
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                w.close()  # type: ignore
            except Exception:
                pass


# -----------------------------
# CLI + main
# -----------------------------
def build_arg_parser() -> argparse.ArgumentParser:
    p = argparse.ArgumentParser(
        prog="baWithPathModel_v3.py",
        description="Model-based BA with soft spline priors + rigid template + tiny slack offsets.",
    )
    p.add_argument("--cameras", required=True, help="Path to cameras.json")
    p.add_argument("--template", required=True, help="Path to mouse template file (mouse3_mesh_shortTail.txt)")
    p.add_argument("--dlc", required=True, help="Path to DLC long-format CSV (dlc_long.csv)")
    p.add_argument("--fps", type=float, default=10.0, help="Frames per second (default: 10)")
    p.add_argument("--out", required=True, help="Output CSV path for estimated 3D coordinates (coords_3d.csv format)")
    p.add_argument("--gt", default=None, help="Optional ground-truth coords_3d.csv to compare against")

    # Diagnostics
    p.add_argument("--quat-order", choices=["auto", "wxyz", "xyzw"], default="auto",
                   help="Quaternion coefficient order for interpreting solver output. "
                        "Use 'auto' (default) to choose the better one if --gt is given.")
    p.add_argument("--allow-mouse-swap", action="store_true",
                   help="When --gt is given, also evaluate a global mouse_id swap and report which is better.")

    # Initialization
    p.add_argument("--init-likelihood-min", type=float, default=0.2,
                   help="Likelihood threshold for triangulation-based initialization (default: 0.2)")

    # Solver
    p.add_argument("--max-iter", type=int, default=200, help="Ceres max iterations (default: 200)")
    p.add_argument("--threads", type=int, default=8, help="Ceres threads (default: 8)")
    p.add_argument("--verbose", action="store_true", help="Print Ceres iteration table")
    p.add_argument("--optimize-cameras", action="store_true", help="Estimate camera extrinsics (default off)")
    p.add_argument("--optimize-intrinsics", action="store_true", help="Estimate camera intrinsics (default off)")

    # Ablation switches
    p.add_argument("--disable-path", action="store_true", help="Disable spline/path priors (set their weights ~0).")
    p.add_argument("--rigid-only", action="store_true", help="Force slack offsets ~0 (pure rigid template).")

    # Video
    p.add_argument("--write-video", action="store_true", help="Render per-camera mp4 videos like mouse_sim2.py.")
    p.add_argument("--video-dir", default=None, help="Directory to write videos into (default: directory of --out).")
    p.add_argument("--video-labels", action="store_true", help="Draw node labels in the video (debug).")

    return p


def main() -> int:
    args = build_arg_parser().parse_args()

    cam_quat, cam_trans, cam_intr = load_cameras_json(args.cameras)
    template_pts = load_template_points(args.template)

    (obs_cam, obs_mouse, obs_joint, obs_frame,
     obs_x, obs_y, obs_l, num_frames) = load_dlc_long_csv(args.dlc)

    init_q, init_t = init_poses_from_triangulation(
        template_pts,
        obs_cam, obs_mouse, obs_joint, obs_frame, obs_x, obs_y, obs_l,
        cam_quat, cam_trans, cam_intr,
        likelihood_min=args.init_likelihood_min,
    )

    wp = default_weight_pack().to_dict()
    wp["knot_interval_frames"] = max(3, int(round(args.fps * 0.3)))

    if args.disable_path:
        wp["sigma_spline_p_mm"] = 1e9
        wp["sigma_spline_R_rad"] = 1e9

    if args.rigid_only:
        tiny = 1e-6
        wp["sigma_delta_mm"] = {j: tiny for j in range(len(JOINTS))}
        wp["sigma_deltadot_mm_per_frame"] = {j: tiny for j in range(len(JOINTS))}

    solver_opts = {
        "max_num_iterations": int(args.max_iter),
        "num_threads": int(args.threads),
        "verbose": bool(args.verbose),
        "optimize_cameras": bool(args.optimize_cameras),
        "optimize_intrinsics": bool(args.optimize_intrinsics),
    }

    out = mouse_ba.solve(
        cam_quat, cam_trans, cam_intr,
        template_pts,
        obs_cam, obs_mouse, obs_joint, obs_frame,
        obs_x, obs_y, obs_l,
        int(num_frames),
        init_q, init_t,
        wp,
        solver_opts,
    )
    print(out["summary"])

    mouse_quat = np.asarray(out["mouse_quat"])
    mouse_trans = np.asarray(out["mouse_trans"])
    slack = np.asarray(out["slack"])

    # Choose quaternion order + optional mouse-id swap using GT if requested
    chosen_order = args.quat_order
    chosen_swap = False

    def eval_config(order: str, do_swap: bool) -> Tuple[float, Dict[str, pd.DataFrame], pd.DataFrame]:
        df = build_estimated_coords_df(template_pts, mouse_quat, mouse_trans, slack,
                                       fps=float(args.fps), quat_order=order, mouse_id_swap=do_swap)
        stats = compare_to_ground_truth(df, args.gt) if args.gt else {}
        rmse = float(stats["overall"]["RMSE_mm"].iloc[0]) if args.gt else float("nan")
        return rmse, stats, df

    stats = None
    est_df = None

    if args.gt and args.quat_order == "auto":
        candidates = []
        for order in ("wxyz", "xyzw"):
            candidates.append((order, False))
            if args.allow_mouse_swap:
                candidates.append((order, True))
        best = None
        for order, do_swap in candidates:
            rmse, st, df = eval_config(order, do_swap)
            if best is None or rmse < best[0]:
                best = (rmse, order, do_swap, st, df)
        assert best is not None
        _, chosen_order, chosen_swap, stats, est_df = best
        print(f"[diagnostic] Selected quat_order={chosen_order}  mouse_id_swap={chosen_swap} based on lowest RMSE.")
    else:
        est_df = build_estimated_coords_df(template_pts, mouse_quat, mouse_trans, slack,
                                           fps=float(args.fps), quat_order=chosen_order, mouse_id_swap=False)
        if args.gt:
            stats = compare_to_ground_truth(est_df, args.gt)

    out_path = Path(args.out)
    out_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    est_df.to_csv(out_path, index=False)
    print(f"Wrote estimated 3D coordinates to: {out_path}")

    if args.gt and stats is not None:
        print("\n=== Accuracy vs ground truth (mm) ===")
        print(stats["overall"].to_string(index=False))
        print("\nMean axis offsets (est - gt) and std:")
        print(stats["offsets"].to_string(index=False))
        print("\nPer-mouse:")
        print(stats["per_mouse"].to_string(index=False))
        print("\nPer-node (worst first):")
        print(stats["per_node"].to_string(index=False))
        gt_df = pd.read_csv(args.gt)
        print(f"\nMatched rows: {len(stats['merged'])} (est={len(est_df)}, gt={len(gt_df)})")

    if args.write_video:
        video_dir = Path(args.video_dir) if args.video_dir else out_path.parent
        if cv2 is None and _VIDEO_BACKEND != "imageio":
            raise RuntimeError("Video requested but neither opencv nor imageio is installed.")
        write_videos(
            cameras_json_path=args.cameras,
            template_path=args.template,
            coords_df=est_df,
            out_dir=video_dir,
            fps=float(args.fps),
            draw_labels=bool(args.video_labels),
        )
        print(f"Wrote videos to: {video_dir}")

    return 0


if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main())

Assistant: Your BA result *converged*; the huge GT error is almost certainly **not** a “Ceres didn’t converge” issue.

Two very plausible explanations:

1) **Quaternion coefficient order mismatch** between what the C++ backend outputs and what the Python script assumes when converting quaternions → rotation matrices.  
   - If the backend stores quaternions as **(x,y,z,w)** (Eigen order) but Python interprets as **(w,x,y,z)**, your *computed* 3D coordinates will be wrong by large rotations → huge GT error, even if the optimization itself is fine.

2) **Mouse identity swap** (global or partial). A global swap is easy to test and sometimes happens if IDs are inconsistent.

To make this diagnostic automatic *and* to add optional video rendering like `mouse_sim2.py`, here’s an updated script.

## New script with auto quaternion-order check + optional mouse swap + video output

[Download baWithPathModel_v3.py](sandbox:/mnt/data/baWithPathModel_v3.py)

### What it adds
- `--quat-order {auto,wxyz,xyzw}`  
  - Default `auto`: if `--gt` is provided, it evaluates both conventions and picks the one with lower RMSE.
- `--allow-mouse-swap`  
  - If set and `--gt` given, it also tests a global mouse-id swap and picks the best.
- `--write-video` (+ `--video-dir`, `--video-labels`)  
  - Produces `cam1_top.mp4`, `cam2_front.mp4`, `cam3_side.mp4` in the specified directory, with cage + skeletons rendered in the same style as `mouse_sim2.py`.

It also prints **mean axis offsets (est−gt)** to catch “everything shifted” cases immediately.

---

## How to run it

Copy it into your `python/` folder:

```bash
cp /path/to/baWithPathModel_v3.py python/baWithPathModel_v3.py
```

Then:

```bash
python baWithPathModel_v3.py \
  --cameras ../cameras.json \
  --template ../mouse3_mesh_shortTail.txt \
  --dlc ../dlc_long.csv \
  --fps 10 \
  --out ../coords_3d_est.csv \
  --gt ../../mouse_sim/out2m_2/coords_3d.csv \
  --allow-mouse-swap \
  --verbose
```

If you want videos:

```bash
python baWithPathModel_v3.py \
  ...same args... \
  --write-video \
  --video-dir ../videos_est
```

### Video dependency
`mouse_sim2.py` uses OpenCV if available; this script does the same.

If you don’t have it in your conda env:
```bash
conda install -c conda-forge opencv
```

---

## Why I think it’s quaternion order (most likely)
Your GT RMSE (~108 mm) is enormous yet the solver reduces cost smoothly and terminates with CONVERGENCE. That pattern is very consistent with: *the solver is fine, but the “export-to-world” conversion is wrong*. A quaternion ordering mismatch will do exactly that.

Run v3 once and it will tell you something like:

- `[diagnostic] Selected quat_order=xyzw ... based on lowest RMSE.`

If RMSE drops from ~108 mm to something like a few mm–cm, we’ve found the real issue.

---

If you run `baWithPathModel_v3.py` and paste the “Selected quat_order=…” line plus the new RMSE table, we can decide the next fix: either adjust the Python export permanently, or (better) make the C++ backend output quaternions in an explicitly documented order.

### How to update your existing `mouseba` environment

From your project root (where `environment.yml` lives), first replace/overwrite `environment.yml` with the updated one, then run:

**Using conda:**
```bash
conda activate mouseba
conda env update -n mouseba -f environment.yml --prune
```

**Using mamba (faster, if you have it):**
```bash
conda activate mouseba
mamba env update -n mouseba -f environment.yml --prune
```

Notes:
- `--prune` removes packages that are no longer listed in the YAML (keeps the env tidy).
- After the update completes, it’s a good idea to refresh the shell’s environment:
  ```bash
  conda deactivate
  conda activate mouseba
  ```

Quick verification:
```bash
python -c "import cv2, imageio; print('video deps ok')"
```

code = r"""#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
code += r'''
"""baWithPathModel_v4.py

Adds on top of v3:
- Fix video JSON parsing bug (remove pandas.read_json usage).
- Adds pose convention diagnostics (body_to_world vs world_to_body) with --pose-mode
  and auto-selection when GT is provided.

This is intended to diagnose large GT errors that may stem from differing SE(3)
pose conventions between backend and export logic.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import sys

from typing import Dict, Tuple, Optional, List

import numpy as np
import pandas as pd
