correction_code = r'''

# -----------------------------
# Color-based identity correction (2 mice)
# -----------------------------
def _parse_mouse_id(individual: str) -> int:
    s = str(individual)
    digits = "".join([c for c in s if c.isdigit()])
    if digits:
        try:
            return int(digits)
        except Exception:
            pass
    # fallback: stable ordering elsewhere
    return -1


def _kmeans2(points: np.ndarray, iters: int = 20) -> np.ndarray:
    """
    Tiny k-means for k=2, returns centers (2,3) in BGR.
    """
    if len(points) < 2:
        raise ValueError("Need >=2 points for kmeans2")

    # init: farthest pair heuristic
    p0 = points[0]
    d = np.sum((points - p0) ** 2, axis=1)
    c1 = points[int(np.argmax(d))]
    d2 = np.sum((points - c1) ** 2, axis=1)
    c0 = points[int(np.argmax(d2))]
    centers = np.stack([c0, c1], axis=0).astype(np.float64)

    for _ in range(iters):
        dist0 = np.sum((points - centers[0]) ** 2, axis=1)
        dist1 = np.sum((points - centers[1]) ** 2, axis=1)
        labels = (dist1 < dist0).astype(np.int32)
        for k in (0, 1):
            sel = points[labels == k]
            if len(sel) > 0:
                centers[k] = np.mean(sel, axis=0)
    return centers


def _pick_separation_frames(df_cam: pd.DataFrame, min_lik: float, k: int) -> List[int]:
    """
    Pick frames where centroids of mouse0 and mouse1 are far apart.
    Uses current 'individual' labels only as a proxy to find separation.
    """
    d = df_cam[df_cam["likelihood"] >= min_lik].copy()
    if d.empty:
        return []
    # map individuals to 0/1 (stable)
    inds = sorted(d["individual"].astype(str).unique().tolist())
    if len(inds) < 2:
        return []
    if len(inds) > 2:
        inds = inds[:2]
    mapping = {inds[0]: 0, inds[1]: 1}
    d["mid"] = d["individual"].astype(str).map(mapping).astype(int)
    g = d.groupby(["frame", "mid"])[["x", "y"]].mean().reset_index()
    g0 = g[g["mid"] == 0].set_index("frame")
    g1 = g[g["mid"] == 1].set_index("frame")
    frames = sorted(list(set(g0.index).intersection(set(g1.index))))
    if not frames:
        return []
    dist = []
    for fr in frames:
        dx = float(g0.loc[fr, "x"] - g1.loc[fr, "x"])
        dy = float(g0.loc[fr, "y"] - g1.loc[fr, "y"])
        dist.append((int(fr), (dx*dx + dy*dy) ** 0.5))
    dist.sort(key=lambda t: t[1], reverse=True)
    return [fr for fr, _ in dist[:k]]


def _median_patch(frame_bgr: np.ndarray, x: float, y: float, r: int) -> Optional[np.ndarray]:
    if not (np.isfinite(x) and np.isfinite(y)):
        return None
    H, W = frame_bgr.shape[:2]
    xi, yi = int(round(x)), int(round(y))
    x0, x1 = max(0, xi - r), min(W, xi + r + 1)
    y0, y1 = max(0, yi - r), min(H, yi + r + 1)
    patch = frame_bgr[y0:y1, x0:x1]
    if patch.size == 0:
        return None
    pix = patch.reshape(-1, 3).astype(np.float64)
    return np.median(pix, axis=0)


def _assign_color_id(
    frame_bgr: np.ndarray,
    x: float, y: float,
    r: int,
    centers_bgr: np.ndarray,     # (2,3): [brown, blue]
    dist_thresh: float,
    min_frac: float,
    min_pixels: int,
    dominance: float,
) -> Tuple[int, float]:
    """
    Returns (color_id, confidence), where color_id in {0,1,-1}
      0 => brown, 1 => blue, -1 => unassigned
    """
    if not (np.isfinite(x) and np.isfinite(y)):
        return -1, 0.0
    H, W = frame_bgr.shape[:2]
    xi, yi = int(round(x)), int(round(y))
    x0, x1 = max(0, xi - r), min(W, xi + r + 1)
    y0, y1 = max(0, yi - r), min(H, yi + r + 1)
    patch = frame_bgr[y0:y1, x0:x1]
    if patch.size == 0:
        return -1, 0.0
    pix = patch.reshape(-1, 3).astype(np.float64)
    n = pix.shape[0]
    if n < min_pixels:
        return -1, 0.0
    thr2 = float(dist_thresh) ** 2
    d0 = np.sum((pix - centers_bgr[0]) ** 2, axis=1)
    d1 = np.sum((pix - centers_bgr[1]) ** 2, axis=1)
    c0 = int(np.sum(d0 <= thr2))
    c1 = int(np.sum(d1 <= thr2))
    best = 0 if c0 >= c1 else 1
    bestc = max(c0, c1)
    otherc = min(c0, c1)
    frac = bestc / max(1, n)
    if frac < min_frac:
        return -1, 0.0
    if bestc < otherc * (1.0 + dominance) and (bestc - otherc) < 5:
        return -1, 0.0
    conf = (bestc - otherc) / max(1, n)
    return best, float(conf)


def correct_identities_for_camera(
    df_cam: pd.DataFrame,
    video_path: str | Path,
    sep_likelihood: float,
    calib_frames: int,
    calib_likelihood: float,
    vote_likelihood: float,
    patch_radius: int,
    color_dist: float,
    min_fur_frac: float,
    min_pixels: int,
    dominance: float,
    drop_on_conflict: bool,
) -> pd.DataFrame:
    """
    Returns corrected df_cam (same columns as input, may drop some conflicting rows).
    """
    df_cam = df_cam.copy()
    df_cam["frame"] = df_cam["frame"].astype(int)

    # stable individual list, expect 2 mice
    inds = sorted(df_cam["individual"].astype(str).unique().tolist())
    if len(inds) != 2:
        print(f"[autoCorrect] Expected 2 individuals, found {inds}. Skipping correction.")
        return df_cam

    # map to numeric id by name order
    ind_to_id = {inds[0]: 0, inds[1]: 1}
    df_cam["mid"] = df_cam["individual"].astype(str).map(ind_to_id).astype(int)

    # choose calibration frames
    cal_frames = _pick_separation_frames(df_cam, min_lik=sep_likelihood, k=calib_frames)
    if len(cal_frames) < 3:
        print("[autoCorrect] Not enough separated frames found; skipping correction.")
        return df_cam.drop(columns=["mid"], errors="ignore")

    cap = cv2.VideoCapture(str(video_path))
    if not cap.isOpened():
        raise RuntimeError(f"Could not open video for correction: {video_path}")

    # prepare df index
    df_cam = df_cam.sort_values("frame").reset_index(drop=True)
    frames_arr = df_cam["frame"].to_numpy(dtype=np.int64)
    nrows = len(df_cam)

    # Step 1: build color prototypes from calibration frames
    exclude_bps = {"tail_tip"}
    cal_set = set(cal_frames)
    samples = []

    idx = 0
    fr = 0
    max_fr = max(cal_frames)
    while True:
        ok, frame = cap.read()
        if not ok or fr > max_fr:
            break
        if fr in cal_set:
            while idx < nrows and frames_arr[idx] < fr:
                idx += 1
            start = idx
            while idx < nrows and frames_arr[idx] == fr:
                idx += 1
            if idx > start:
                rows = df_cam.iloc[start:idx]
                rows = rows[(rows["likelihood"] >= calib_likelihood) & (~rows["bodypart"].astype(str).isin(exclude_bps))]
                for r in rows.itertuples(index=False):
                    c = _median_patch(frame, float(r.x), float(r.y), patch_radius)
                    if c is not None and np.all(np.isfinite(c)):
                        samples.append(c)
        fr += 1

    cap.release()

    if len(samples) < 20:
        print("[autoCorrect] Too few color samples; skipping correction.")
        return df_cam.drop(columns=["mid"], errors="ignore")

    pts = np.stack(samples, axis=0)
    centers = _kmeans2(pts, iters=25)  # (2,3) BGR

    # decide brown vs blue
    # brown: R > B  -> channel2 > channel0
    brown_idx = 0 if centers[0, 2] >= centers[0, 0] else 1
    blue_idx = 1 - brown_idx
    centers_bgr = np.stack([centers[brown_idx], centers[blue_idx]], axis=0)
    print(f"[autoCorrect] Prototypes (BGR): brown~{centers_bgr[0].round(1).tolist()}  blue~{centers_bgr[1].round(1).tolist()}")

    # Step 2: color assignment for each row (second pass)
    cap = cv2.VideoCapture(str(video_path))
    if not cap.isOpened():
        raise RuntimeError(f"Could not open video for correction (pass2): {video_path}")

    df_cam["color_id"] = -1
    df_cam["color_conf"] = 0.0

    idx = 0
    fr = 0
    while True:
        ok, frame = cap.read()
        if not ok:
            break

        while idx < nrows and frames_arr[idx] < fr:
            idx += 1
        start = idx
        while idx < nrows and frames_arr[idx] == fr:
            idx += 1
        if idx > start:
            sub = df_cam.iloc[start:idx]
            for ridx, r in zip(range(start, idx), sub.itertuples(index=False)):
                if float(r.likelihood) < vote_likelihood:
                    continue
                cid, conf = _assign_color_id(
                    frame, float(r.x), float(r.y),
                    patch_radius, centers_bgr,
                    color_dist, min_fur_frac, min_pixels, dominance
                )
                if cid != -1:
                    df_cam.at[ridx, "color_id"] = cid
                    df_cam.at[ridx, "color_conf"] = conf
        fr += 1

    cap.release()

    # Step 3: frame-level swap (majority vote)
    votes = df_cam[(df_cam["color_id"] >= 0) & (df_cam["likelihood"] >= vote_likelihood)]
    if votes.empty:
        print("[autoCorrect] No usable color votes; skipping correction.")
        return df_cam.drop(columns=["mid"], errors="ignore")

    # score per frame: noswap vs swap
    def score_frame(x: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:
        mid = x["mid"].to_numpy(dtype=int)
        cid = x["color_id"].to_numpy(dtype=int)
        nos = int(np.sum(cid == mid))
        sw = int(np.sum(cid == (1 - mid)))
        return pd.Series({"noswap": nos, "swap": sw})

    scores = votes.groupby("frame").apply(score_frame).reset_index()
    swap_frames = set(scores[scores["swap"] > scores["noswap"]]["frame"].astype(int).tolist())
    if swap_frames:
        print(f"[autoCorrect] Frame-level swaps: {len(swap_frames)} frames.")

    df_cam["mid_corr"] = df_cam["mid"].astype(int)
    m = df_cam["frame"].isin(swap_frames)
    df_cam.loc[m, "mid_corr"] = 1 - df_cam.loc[m, "mid_corr"]

    # Step 4: body-part-level correction
    keep = np.ones(len(df_cam), dtype=bool)

    # process each (frame, bodypart)
    for (fr, bp), grp in df_cam.groupby(["frame", "bodypart"]):
        # choose best row per corrected mid (if duplicates exist)
        rows = {}
        for mid in (0, 1):
            sub = grp[grp["mid_corr"] == mid]
            if sub.empty:
                continue
            rows[mid] = sub.sort_values("likelihood", ascending=False).iloc[0]

        if not rows:
            continue

        # both present and both say swap -> swap them
        if 0 in rows and 1 in rows:
            r0, r1 = rows[0], rows[1]
            if int(r0["color_id"]) == 1 and int(r1["color_id"]) == 0:
                df_cam.at[r0.name, "mid_corr"] = 1
                df_cam.at[r1.name, "mid_corr"] = 0
                continue

        # otherwise: if one wants to move
        for mid, r in rows.items():
            cid = int(r["color_id"])
            if cid < 0:
                continue
            if cid == mid:
                continue
            target_mid = cid
            if target_mid not in rows:
                # reassign
                df_cam.at[r.name, "mid_corr"] = target_mid
            else:
                # conflict
                if drop_on_conflict:
                    keep[r.name] = False

    df_cam = df_cam[keep].copy()

    # rewrite individuals to canonical mouse0/mouse1 so overlay colors stay stable
    df_cam["individual"] = df_cam["mid_corr"].astype(int).map(lambda m: f"mouse{m}")

    return df_cam.drop(columns=["mid", "mid_corr"], errors="ignore")

'''

patched = src[:pos] + correction_code + src[pos:]

Assistant: Implemented. Here’s the extended program that performs the **color-based identity + body-part correction** exactly along your steps (frame-level majority check + safe per-part switching with conflict handling), while keeping the same overlay style and the `--joinedVideo` mosaic feature.

[Download overlay_dlc_on_videos_v3.py](sandbox:/mnt/data/overlay_dlc_on_videos_v3.py)

---

## What it adds

### Identity & part correction (`--autoCorrect`)
Per camera (top/front/side), it:

1) **Finds separation frames** (largest centroid distance between the two mice, using high-likelihood points).
2) **Learns two fur color prototypes** (k=2 clustering on median patch colors):
   - prototype with **R > B** → **brown** → mouse0  
   - other prototype → **blue** → mouse1
3) For each detection row, **tries to assign a color-based mouse ID** from a local patch.
   - If uncertain (too few “fur-like” pixels), leaves it unassigned.
4) **Frame-level identity swap** if the majority of confident part-votes disagree with DLC IDs.
5) **Part-level correction**:
   - if both mice’s same bodypart are confidently swapped → swap them
   - if only one wants to move but the target already has that bodypart:
     - by default: do nothing
     - with `--drop-on-conflict`: **drop** the “leaving” row (your recommended safe behavior)

Optionally writes a corrected CSV to `--dlcOut`.

---

## How to run

### Produce corrected overlay videos + joined mosaic + corrected CSV
```bash
python overlay_dlc_on_videos_v3.py \
  --dlc ../dlc_long.csv \
  --topIn top.mp4 --frontIn front.mp4 --sideIn side.mp4 \
  --topOut top_anno.mp4 --frontOut front_anno.mp4 --sideOut side_anno.mp4 \
  --joinedVideo joined_anno.mp4 \
  --template ../mouse3_mesh_shortTail.txt \
  --likelihood-min 0.2 \
  --autoCorrect \
  --drop-on-conflict \
  --dlcOut ../dlc_long_corrected.csv
```

### Useful debugging option
```bash
--draw-labels
```
This prints `mouse#:bodypart` next to points to visually confirm the fixes.

---

## Key knobs (defaults are conservative)

- `--sep-likelihood 0.7` : used to find “mice clearly separated” frames  
- `--calib-frames 25` : how many separation frames used for color prototypes  
- `--calib-likelihood 0.85` : only very confident detections used for color calibration  
- `--vote-likelihood 0.5` : only fairly confident detections vote / get corrected  
- `--patch-radius 6` : patch is (2r+1)² = 13×13  
- `--color-dist 35` : color distance threshold in BGR space for “fur-like” pixels  
- `--min-fur-frac 0.08` : must have at least this fraction of fur-like pixels  
- `--drop-on-conflict` : if a part wants to switch but target already has it → drop it

If you see too few corrections: lower `--vote-likelihood` to ~0.3 and/or raise `--patch-radius` to 8.  
If you see over-corrections: increase `--min-fur-frac` to ~0.12 or decrease `--color-dist` to ~28.

- whether `dlc_long_corrected.csv` looks improved in the overlay,

then we can tune the thresholds quickly (especially `color-dist` and `min-fur-frac`) to reduce false assignments near tails / background.

User: Please add an option to manually define mouse0 and mouse1 bgr vectors.

In the current version the correction does not work at all. In particular, the RGB values of the mice fur are not determined correctly. 

There may be a good chance to find the fur color at the framewise center of gravity of a mouse's extracted paws. A stable value could be found by computing the median of these center of gravity vector components (r, g, b). But due to the identity flips first the center of gravity vectors have to be clustered into two clusters in color space (disregarding the IDs). Then the median computation of the cluster members of the two clusters could be done for each color component, eg. red.

Assistant: from pathlib import Path
import os, stat, re, textwrap, json

src = Path("/mnt/data/overlay_dlc_on_videos_v3.py").read_text(encoding="utf-8")

# We'll produce a v4 by editing the correction section:
# 1) Add parse_bgr helper near top (after imports)
# 2) Modify correct_identities_for_camera to accept manual_bgr0/bgr1 and use paw-centroid sampling + cluster medians.
# Easiest: replace the entire "Color-based identity correction (2 mice)" section with a new one.

# Find the section start and end by markers.
start_marker = "# -----------------------------\n# Color-based identity correction (2 mice)\n"
start = src.find(start_marker)
assert start != -1

# End marker: next "# -----------------------------\n# Main" maybe; we'll locate that.
end_marker = "# -----------------------------\n# Main\n"
end = src.find(end_marker, start)
assert end != -1

before = src[:start]
after = src[end:]  # includes main onwards

new_corr = r"""# -----------------------------
# Color-based identity correction (2 mice)
# -----------------------------
def parse_bgr_triplet(s: str) -> np.ndarray:
    """
    Parse 'b,g,r' or 'b g r' into float64 array shape (3,).
    """
    if s is None:
        raise ValueError("Empty BGR string")
    t = str(s).strip().replace(",", " ").split()
    if len(t) != 3:
        raise ValueError(f"Expected 3 values for BGR, got: {s!r}")
    return np.array([float(t[0]), float(t[1]), float(t[2])], dtype=np.float64)


def _kmeans2(points: np.ndarray, iters: int = 25) -> Tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
    """
    Small kmeans for k=2. Returns (centers (2,3), labels (N,)).
    """
    if len(points) < 2:
        raise ValueError("Need >=2 points for kmeans2")
    pts = points.astype(np.float64)

    # init: farthest pair heuristic
    p0 = pts[0]
    d = np.sum((pts - p0) ** 2, axis=1)
    c1 = pts[int(np.argmax(d))]
    d2 = np.sum((pts - c1) ** 2, axis=1)
    c0 = pts[int(np.argmax(d2))]
    centers = np.stack([c0, c1], axis=0).astype(np.float64)

    labels = np.zeros(len(pts), dtype=np.int32)
    for _ in range(iters):
        dist0 = np.sum((pts - centers[0]) ** 2, axis=1)
        dist1 = np.sum((pts - centers[1]) ** 2, axis=1)
        labels = (dist1 < dist0).astype(np.int32)
        for k in (0, 1):
            sel = pts[labels == k]
            if len(sel) > 0:
                centers[k] = np.mean(sel, axis=0)

    # final labels
    dist0 = np.sum((pts - centers[0]) ** 2, axis=1)
    dist1 = np.sum((pts - centers[1]) ** 2, axis=1)
    labels = (dist1 < dist0).astype(np.int32)
    return centers, labels


def _pick_separation_frames(df_cam: pd.DataFrame, min_lik: float, k: int) -> List[int]:
    """
    Pick frames where the two labeled individuals are far apart (centroid distance).
    This does NOT assume labels are stable; it only uses them to find separation.
    """
    d = df_cam[df_cam["likelihood"] >= min_lik].copy()
    if d.empty:
        return []
    inds = sorted(d["individual"].astype(str).unique().tolist())
    if len(inds) != 2:
        return []
    mapping = {inds[0]: 0, inds[1]: 1}
    d["mid"] = d["individual"].astype(str).map(mapping).astype(int)
    g = d.groupby(["frame", "mid"])[["x", "y"]].mean().reset_index()
    g0 = g[g["mid"] == 0].set_index("frame")
    g1 = g[g["mid"] == 1].set_index("frame")
    frames = sorted(list(set(g0.index).intersection(set(g1.index))))
    if not frames:
        return []
    dist = []
    for fr in frames:
        dx = float(g0.loc[fr, "x"] - g1.loc[fr, "x"])
        dy = float(g0.loc[fr, "y"] - g1.loc[fr, "y"])
        dist.append((int(fr), (dx*dx + dy*dy) ** 0.5))
    dist.sort(key=lambda t: t[1], reverse=True)
    return [fr for fr, _ in dist[:k]]


def _median_patch(frame_bgr: np.ndarray, x: float, y: float, r: int) -> Optional[np.ndarray]:
    if not (np.isfinite(x) and np.isfinite(y)):
        return None
    H, W = frame_bgr.shape[:2]
    xi, yi = int(round(x)), int(round(y))
    x0, x1 = max(0, xi - r), min(W, xi + r + 1)
    y0, y1 = max(0, yi - r), min(H, yi + r + 1)
    patch = frame_bgr[y0:y1, x0:x1]
    if patch.size == 0:
        return None
    pix = patch.reshape(-1, 3).astype(np.float64)
    return np.median(pix, axis=0)


def _assign_color_id(
    frame_bgr: np.ndarray,
    x: float, y: float,
    r: int,
    proto0_bgr: np.ndarray,  # mouse0
    proto1_bgr: np.ndarray,  # mouse1
    dist_thresh: float,
    min_frac: float,
    min_pixels: int,
    dominance: float,
) -> Tuple[int, float]:
    """
    Returns (assigned_id in {0,1,-1}, confidence).
    Looks for pixels in the patch close to either prototype.
    """
    if not (np.isfinite(x) and np.isfinite(y)):
        return -1, 0.0
    H, W = frame_bgr.shape[:2]
    xi, yi = int(round(x)), int(round(y))
    x0, x1 = max(0, xi - r), min(W, xi + r + 1)
    y0, y1 = max(0, yi - r), min(H, yi + r + 1)
    patch = frame_bgr[y0:y1, x0:x1]
    if patch.size == 0:
        return -1, 0.0
    pix = patch.reshape(-1, 3).astype(np.float64)
    n = pix.shape[0]
    if n < min_pixels:
        return -1, 0.0
    thr2 = float(dist_thresh) ** 2
    d0 = np.sum((pix - proto0_bgr) ** 2, axis=1)
    d1 = np.sum((pix - proto1_bgr) ** 2, axis=1)
    c0 = int(np.sum(d0 <= thr2))
    c1 = int(np.sum(d1 <= thr2))
    best = 0 if c0 >= c1 else 1
    bestc = max(c0, c1)
    otherc = min(c0, c1)
    frac = bestc / max(1, n)
    if frac < min_frac:
        return -1, 0.0
    if bestc < otherc * (1.0 + dominance) and (bestc - otherc) < 5:
        return -1, 0.0
    conf = (bestc - otherc) / max(1, n)
    return best, float(conf)


def _paw_centroid(rows: pd.DataFrame, paw_parts: List[str], min_lik: float) -> Optional[Tuple[float, float]]:
    sub = rows[(rows["bodypart"].astype(str).isin(paw_parts)) & (rows["likelihood"] >= min_lik)]
    if len(sub) < 2:
        return None
    return float(sub["x"].mean()), float(sub["y"].mean())


def _fallback_centroid(rows: pd.DataFrame, parts: List[str], min_lik: float) -> Optional[Tuple[float, float]]:
    sub = rows[(rows["bodypart"].astype(str).isin(parts)) & (rows["likelihood"] >= min_lik)]
    if len(sub) < 2:
        return None
    return float(sub["x"].mean()), float(sub["y"].mean())


def estimate_fur_prototypes_from_paw_cog(
    df_cam: pd.DataFrame,
    video_path: str | Path,
    sep_frames: List[int],
    patch_radius: int,
    calib_likelihood: float,
) -> Tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
    """
    Returns (proto0_bgr, proto1_bgr) for mouse0 and mouse1.
    Uses per-frame paw centroid samples for BOTH labeled individuals, then clusters in color space ignoring IDs.
    Then assigns the 'brown' cluster (R > B) to mouse0 and the 'blue' cluster to mouse1.
    """
    paw_parts = ["left_front_paw", "right_front_paw", "left_hind_paw", "right_hind_paw"]
    fallback_parts = ["head", "tail_root", "nose_tip", "left_ear_tip", "right_ear_tip"]

    inds = sorted(df_cam["individual"].astype(str).unique().tolist())
    if len(inds) != 2:
        raise ValueError(f"Expected 2 individuals, got: {inds}")

    df_cam = df_cam.copy()
    df_cam["frame"] = df_cam["frame"].astype(int)

    cap = cv2.VideoCapture(str(video_path))
    if not cap.isOpened():
        raise RuntimeError(f"Could not open video for calibration: {video_path}")

    # index df by frame for quick slicing
    df_cam = df_cam.sort_values("frame").reset_index(drop=True)
    frames_arr = df_cam["frame"].to_numpy(dtype=np.int64)
    nrows = len(df_cam)
    idx = 0

    sep_set = set(sep_frames)
    max_fr = max(sep_frames) if sep_frames else -1
    samples = []

    fr = 0
    while True:
        ok, frame = cap.read()
        if not ok:
            break
        if max_fr >= 0 and fr > max_fr:
            break

        if fr in sep_set:
            while idx < nrows and frames_arr[idx] < fr:
                idx += 1
            start = idx
            while idx < nrows and frames_arr[idx] == fr:
                idx += 1
            if idx > start:
                rows_fr = df_cam.iloc[start:idx]
                for ind in inds:
                    rows_ind = rows_fr[rows_fr["individual"].astype(str) == ind]
                    cog = _paw_centroid(rows_ind, paw_parts, calib_likelihood)
                    if cog is None:
                        cog = _fallback_centroid(rows_ind, fallback_parts, calib_likelihood)
                    if cog is None:
                        continue
                    c = _median_patch(frame, cog[0], cog[1], patch_radius)
                    if c is not None and np.all(np.isfinite(c)):
                        samples.append(c)

        fr += 1

    cap.release()

    if len(samples) < 20:
        raise RuntimeError("Too few color samples from paw COG for calibration (need >=20).")

    pts = np.stack(samples, axis=0)  # (N,3)

    # cluster ignoring IDs
    _, labels = _kmeans2(pts, iters=30)

    # robust prototype per cluster: channel-wise median
    protoA = np.median(pts[labels == 0], axis=0)
    protoB = np.median(pts[labels == 1], axis=0)

    # Decide which is brown (mouse0): R > B  => proto[2] > proto[0] in BGR
    if protoA[2] >= protoA[0] and protoB[2] < protoB[0]:
        proto0, proto1 = protoA, protoB
    elif protoB[2] >= protoB[0] and protoA[2] < protoA[0]:
        proto0, proto1 = protoB, protoA
    else:
        # fallback: use the larger (R-B) as brown
        if (protoA[2] - protoA[0]) >= (protoB[2] - protoB[0]):
            proto0, proto1 = protoA, protoB
        else:
            proto0, proto1 = protoB, protoA

    return proto0.astype(np.float64), proto1.astype(np.float64)


def correct_identities_for_camera(
    df_cam: pd.DataFrame,
    video_path: str | Path,
    sep_likelihood: float,
    calib_frames: int,
    calib_likelihood: float,
    vote_likelihood: float,
    patch_radius: int,
    color_dist: float,
    min_fur_frac: float,
    min_pixels: int,
    dominance: float,
    drop_on_conflict: bool,
    manual_mouse0_bgr: Optional[np.ndarray] = None,
    manual_mouse1_bgr: Optional[np.ndarray] = None,
) -> pd.DataFrame:
    """
    Implements steps 1-4 as described by the user.

    If manual_mouse{0,1}_bgr are provided, uses them directly.
    Otherwise, estimates prototypes from paw centroid colors (clustered in color space ignoring IDs).
    """
    df_cam = df_cam.copy()
    df_cam["frame"] = df_cam["frame"].astype(int)

    inds = sorted(df_cam["individual"].astype(str).unique().tolist())
    if len(inds) != 2:
        print(f"[autoCorrect] Expected 2 individuals, found {inds}. Skipping correction.")
        return df_cam

    # Map current labels to a working mid in {0,1} (only for comparison / frame swap decision).
    ind_to_mid = {inds[0]: 0, inds[1]: 1}
    df_cam["mid"] = df_cam["individual"].astype(str).map(ind_to_mid).astype(int)

    # Step 1: prototypes
    if manual_mouse0_bgr is not None and manual_mouse1_bgr is not None:
        proto0_bgr = manual_mouse0_bgr.astype(np.float64)
        proto1_bgr = manual_mouse1_bgr.astype(np.float64)
        print(f"[autoCorrect] Using MANUAL prototypes (BGR): mouse0~{proto0_bgr.round(1).tolist()} mouse1~{proto1_bgr.round(1).tolist()}")
    else:
        sep_frames = _pick_separation_frames(df_cam, min_lik=sep_likelihood, k=calib_frames)
        if len(sep_frames) < 3:
            print("[autoCorrect] Not enough separated frames found; skipping correction.")
            return df_cam.drop(columns=["mid"], errors="ignore")
        proto0_bgr, proto1_bgr = estimate_fur_prototypes_from_paw_cog(
            df_cam=df_cam.drop(columns=["mid"], errors="ignore"),
            video_path=video_path,
            sep_frames=sep_frames,
            patch_radius=patch_radius,
            calib_likelihood=calib_likelihood,
        )
        print(f"[autoCorrect] Estimated prototypes (BGR): mouse0(brown)~{proto0_bgr.round(1).tolist()} mouse1(blue)~{proto1_bgr.round(1).tolist()}")

    # Step 2: per-row color assignment
    cap = cv2.VideoCapture(str(video_path))
    if not cap.isOpened():
        raise RuntimeError(f"Could not open video for correction: {video_path}")

    df_cam = df_cam.sort_values("frame").reset_index(drop=True)
    frames_arr = df_cam["frame"].to_numpy(dtype=np.int64)
    nrows = len(df_cam)

    df_cam["color_id"] = -1
    df_cam["color_conf"] = 0.0

    idx = 0
    fr = 0
    while True:
        ok, frame = cap.read()
        if not ok:
            break

        while idx < nrows and frames_arr[idx] < fr:
            idx += 1
        start = idx
        while idx < nrows and frames_arr[idx] == fr:
            idx += 1
        if idx > start:
            sub = df_cam.iloc[start:idx]
            for ridx, r in zip(range(start, idx), sub.itertuples(index=False)):
                if float(r.likelihood) < vote_likelihood:
                    continue
                cid, conf = _assign_color_id(
                    frame,
                    float(r.x), float(r.y),
                    patch_radius,
                    proto0_bgr, proto1_bgr,
                    color_dist, min_fur_frac, min_pixels, dominance
                )
                if cid != -1:
                    df_cam.at[ridx, "color_id"] = cid
                    df_cam.at[ridx, "color_conf"] = conf
        fr += 1

    cap.release()

    # Step 3: frame-level swap based on majority agreement with DLC IDs
    votes = df_cam[(df_cam["color_id"] >= 0) & (df_cam["likelihood"] >= vote_likelihood)]
    if votes.empty:
        print("[autoCorrect] No usable color votes; skipping correction.")
        return df_cam.drop(columns=["mid"], errors="ignore")

    def score_frame(x: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:
        mid = x["mid"].to_numpy(dtype=int)
        cid = x["color_id"].to_numpy(dtype=int)
        nos = int(np.sum(cid == mid))
        sw = int(np.sum(cid == (1 - mid)))
        return pd.Series({"noswap": nos, "swap": sw})

    scores = votes.groupby("frame").apply(score_frame).reset_index()
    swap_frames = set(scores[scores["swap"] > scores["noswap"]]["frame"].astype(int).tolist())
    if swap_frames:
        print(f"[autoCorrect] Frame-level swaps: {len(swap_frames)} frames.")

    df_cam["mid_corr"] = df_cam["mid"].astype(int)
    m = df_cam["frame"].isin(swap_frames)
    df_cam.loc[m, "mid_corr"] = 1 - df_cam.loc[m, "mid_corr"]

    # Step 4: part-level correction with safe handling
    keep = np.ones(len(df_cam), dtype=bool)

    for (fr, bp), grp in df_cam.groupby(["frame", "bodypart"]):
        # choose best row per corrected mid (in case of duplicates)
        rows = {}
        for mid in (0, 1):
            sub = grp[grp["mid_corr"] == mid]
            if sub.empty:
                continue
            rows[mid] = sub.sort_values("likelihood", ascending=False).iloc[0]

        if not rows:
            continue

        # if both present and both confidently swapped -> swap them
        if 0 in rows and 1 in rows:
            r0, r1 = rows[0], rows[1]
            if int(r0["color_id"]) == 1 and int(r1["color_id"]) == 0:
                df_cam.at[r0.name, "mid_corr"] = 1
                df_cam.at[r1.name, "mid_corr"] = 0
                continue

        # otherwise handle individual moves
        for mid, r in rows.items():
            cid = int(r["color_id"])
            if cid < 0:
                continue
            if cid == mid:
                continue
            target = cid
            if target not in rows:
                # target missing -> reassign
                df_cam.at[r.name, "mid_corr"] = target
            else:
                # target already has it -> conflict
                if drop_on_conflict:
                    keep[r.name] = False

    df_cam = df_cam[keep].copy()

    # Rewrite individuals to canonical names mouse0/mouse1 for consistency
    df_cam["individual"] = df_cam["mid_corr"].astype(int).map(lambda m: f"mouse{m}")

    return df_cam.drop(columns=["mid", "mid_corr"], errors="ignore")
"""

Assistant: from pathlib import Path
import os, stat, re

# Read existing v3
src = Path("/mnt/data/overlay_dlc_on_videos_v3.py").read_text(encoding="utf-8")

start_marker = "# -----------------------------\n# Color-based identity correction (2 mice)\n"
start = src.find(start_marker)
if start == -1:
    raise RuntimeError("Could not find correction section start marker.")
end_marker = "# -----------------------------\n# Main\n"
end = src.find(end_marker, start)
if end == -1:
    raise RuntimeError("Could not find correction section end marker.")

before = src[:start]
after = src[end:]

new_corr = """# -----------------------------
# Color-based identity correction (2 mice)
# -----------------------------
def parse_bgr_triplet(s: str) -> np.ndarray:
    \"\"\"Parse 'b,g,r' or 'b g r' into float64 array shape (3,).\"\"\"
    if s is None:
        raise ValueError("Empty BGR string")
    t = str(s).strip().replace(",", " ").split()
    if len(t) != 3:
        raise ValueError(f"Expected 3 values for BGR, got: {s!r}")
    return np.array([float(t[0]), float(t[1]), float(t[2])], dtype=np.float64)


def _kmeans2(points: np.ndarray, iters: int = 25) -> Tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
    \"\"\"Small kmeans for k=2. Returns (centers (2,3), labels (N,)).\"\"\"
    if len(points) < 2:
        raise ValueError("Need >=2 points for kmeans2")
    pts = points.astype(np.float64)

    # init: farthest pair heuristic
    p0 = pts[0]
    d = np.sum((pts - p0) ** 2, axis=1)
    c1 = pts[int(np.argmax(d))]
    d2 = np.sum((pts - c1) ** 2, axis=1)
    c0 = pts[int(np.argmax(d2))]
    centers = np.stack([c0, c1], axis=0).astype(np.float64)

    labels = np.zeros(len(pts), dtype=np.int32)
    for _ in range(iters):
        dist0 = np.sum((pts - centers[0]) ** 2, axis=1)
        dist1 = np.sum((pts - centers[1]) ** 2, axis=1)
        labels = (dist1 < dist0).astype(np.int32)
        for k in (0, 1):
            sel = pts[labels == k]
            if len(sel) > 0:
                centers[k] = np.mean(sel, axis=0)

    dist0 = np.sum((pts - centers[0]) ** 2, axis=1)
    dist1 = np.sum((pts - centers[1]) ** 2, axis=1)
    labels = (dist1 < dist0).astype(np.int32)
    return centers, labels


def _pick_separation_frames(df_cam: pd.DataFrame, min_lik: float, k: int) -> List[int]:
    \"\"\"Pick frames where the two labeled individuals are far apart (centroid distance).\"\"\"
    d = df_cam[df_cam["likelihood"] >= min_lik].copy()
    if d.empty:
        return []
    inds = sorted(d["individual"].astype(str).unique().tolist())
    if len(inds) != 2:
        return []
    mapping = {inds[0]: 0, inds[1]: 1}
    d["mid_tmp"] = d["individual"].astype(str).map(mapping).astype(int)
    g = d.groupby(["frame", "mid_tmp"])[["x", "y"]].mean().reset_index()
    g0 = g[g["mid_tmp"] == 0].set_index("frame")
    g1 = g[g["mid_tmp"] == 1].set_index("frame")
    frames = sorted(list(set(g0.index).intersection(set(g1.index))))
    if not frames:
        return []
    dist = []
    for fr in frames:
        dx = float(g0.loc[fr, "x"] - g1.loc[fr, "x"])
        dy = float(g0.loc[fr, "y"] - g1.loc[fr, "y"])
        dist.append((int(fr), (dx*dx + dy*dy) ** 0.5))
    dist.sort(key=lambda t: t[1], reverse=True)
    return [fr for fr, _ in dist[:k]]


def _median_patch(frame_bgr: np.ndarray, x: float, y: float, r: int) -> Optional[np.ndarray]:
    if not (np.isfinite(x) and np.isfinite(y)):
        return None
    H, W = frame_bgr.shape[:2]
    xi, yi = int(round(x)), int(round(y))
    x0, x1 = max(0, xi - r), min(W, xi + r + 1)
    y0, y1 = max(0, yi - r), min(H, yi + r + 1)
    patch = frame_bgr[y0:y1, x0:x1]
    if patch.size == 0:
        return None
    pix = patch.reshape(-1, 3).astype(np.float64)
    return np.median(pix, axis=0)


def _assign_color_id(
    frame_bgr: np.ndarray,
    x: float, y: float,
    r: int,
    proto0_bgr: np.ndarray,  # mouse0
    proto1_bgr: np.ndarray,  # mouse1
    dist_thresh: float,
    min_frac: float,
    min_pixels: int,
    dominance: float,
) -> Tuple[int, float]:
    \"\"\"Return (assigned_id in {0,1,-1}, confidence).\"\"\"
    if not (np.isfinite(x) and np.isfinite(y)):
        return -1, 0.0
    H, W = frame_bgr.shape[:2]
    xi, yi = int(round(x)), int(round(y))
    x0, x1 = max(0, xi - r), min(W, xi + r + 1)
    y0, y1 = max(0, yi - r), min(H, yi + r + 1)
    patch = frame_bgr[y0:y1, x0:x1]
    if patch.size == 0:
        return -1, 0.0
    pix = patch.reshape(-1, 3).astype(np.float64)
    n = pix.shape[0]
    if n < min_pixels:
        return -1, 0.0
    thr2 = float(dist_thresh) ** 2
    d0 = np.sum((pix - proto0_bgr) ** 2, axis=1)
    d1 = np.sum((pix - proto1_bgr) ** 2, axis=1)
    c0 = int(np.sum(d0 <= thr2))
    c1 = int(np.sum(d1 <= thr2))
    best = 0 if c0 >= c1 else 1
    bestc = max(c0, c1)
    otherc = min(c0, c1)
    frac = bestc / max(1, n)
    if frac < min_frac:
        return -1, 0.0
    if bestc < otherc * (1.0 + dominance) and (bestc - otherc) < 5:
        return -1, 0.0
    conf = (bestc - otherc) / max(1, n)
    return best, float(conf)


def _paw_centroid(rows: pd.DataFrame, paw_parts: List[str], min_lik: float) -> Optional[Tuple[float, float]]:
    sub = rows[(rows["bodypart"].astype(str).isin(paw_parts)) & (rows["likelihood"] >= min_lik)]
    if len(sub) < 2:
        return None
    return float(sub["x"].mean()), float(sub["y"].mean())


def _fallback_centroid(rows: pd.DataFrame, parts: List[str], min_lik: float) -> Optional[Tuple[float, float]]:
    sub = rows[(rows["bodypart"].astype(str).isin(parts)) & (rows["likelihood"] >= min_lik)]
    if len(sub) < 2:
        return None
    return float(sub["x"].mean()), float(sub["y"].mean())


def estimate_fur_prototypes_from_paw_cog(
    df_cam: pd.DataFrame,
    video_path: str | Path,
    sep_frames: List[int],
    patch_radius: int,
    calib_likelihood: float,
) -> Tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
    \"\"\"
    Estimate (mouse0_bgr, mouse1_bgr) using the median color around the
    framewise center-of-gravity of paws, collected for BOTH labeled mice,
    then clustered into two clusters in color space (ignoring IDs).
    The cluster with R>B (in BGR: channel2 > channel0) is assigned to mouse0 (brown).
    \"\"\"
    paw_parts = ["left_front_paw", "right_front_paw", "left_hind_paw", "right_hind_paw"]
    fallback_parts = ["head", "tail_root", "nose_tip", "left_ear_tip", "right_ear_tip"]

    inds = sorted(df_cam["individual"].astype(str).unique().tolist())
    if len(inds) != 2:
        raise ValueError(f"Expected 2 individuals, got: {inds}")

    df_cam = df_cam.copy()
    df_cam["frame"] = df_cam["frame"].astype(int)

    cap = cv2.VideoCapture(str(video_path))
    if not cap.isOpened():
        raise RuntimeError(f"Could not open video for calibration: {video_path}")

    df_cam = df_cam.sort_values("frame").reset_index(drop=True)
    frames_arr = df_cam["frame"].to_numpy(dtype=np.int64)
    nrows = len(df_cam)
    idx = 0

    sep_set = set(sep_frames)
    max_fr = max(sep_frames) if sep_frames else -1
    samples = []

    fr = 0
    while True:
        ok, frame = cap.read()
        if not ok:
            break
        if max_fr >= 0 and fr > max_fr:
            break

        if fr in sep_set:
            while idx < nrows and frames_arr[idx] < fr:
                idx += 1
            start = idx
            while idx < nrows and frames_arr[idx] == fr:
                idx += 1
            if idx > start:
                rows_fr = df_cam.iloc[start:idx]
                for ind in inds:
                    rows_ind = rows_fr[rows_fr["individual"].astype(str) == ind]
                    cog = _paw_centroid(rows_ind, paw_parts, calib_likelihood)
                    if cog is None:
                        cog = _fallback_centroid(rows_ind, fallback_parts, calib_likelihood)
                    if cog is None:
                        continue
                    c = _median_patch(frame, cog[0], cog[1], patch_radius)
                    if c is not None and np.all(np.isfinite(c)):
                        samples.append(c)
        fr += 1

    cap.release()

    if len(samples) < 20:
        raise RuntimeError("Too few color samples for calibration (need >=20).")

    pts = np.stack(samples, axis=0)
    _, labels = _kmeans2(pts, iters=30)

    protoA = np.median(pts[labels == 0], axis=0)
    protoB = np.median(pts[labels == 1], axis=0)

    # brown (mouse0): R > B  (BGR: proto[2] > proto[0])
    if (protoA[2] - protoA[0]) >= (protoB[2] - protoB[0]):
        cand_brown, cand_blue = protoA, protoB
    else:
        cand_brown, cand_blue = protoB, protoA

    return cand_brown.astype(np.float64), cand_blue.astype(np.float64)


def correct_identities_for_camera(
    df_cam: pd.DataFrame,
    video_path: str | Path,
    sep_likelihood: float,
    calib_frames: int,
    calib_likelihood: float,
    vote_likelihood: float,
    patch_radius: int,
    color_dist: float,
    min_fur_frac: float,
    min_pixels: int,
    dominance: float,
    drop_on_conflict: bool,
    manual_mouse0_bgr: Optional[np.ndarray] = None,
    manual_mouse1_bgr: Optional[np.ndarray] = None,
) -> pd.DataFrame:
    \"\"\"
    Step 3: majority vote per frame -> swap if needed.
    Step 4: safe per-bodypart reassignment or drop on conflict.
    \"\"\"
    df_cam = df_cam.copy()
    df_cam["frame"] = df_cam["frame"].astype(int)

    inds = sorted(df_cam["individual"].astype(str).unique().tolist())
    if len(inds) != 2:
        print(f"[autoCorrect] Expected 2 individuals, found {inds}. Skipping correction.")
        return df_cam

    ind_to_mid = {inds[0]: 0, inds[1]: 1}
    df_cam["mid"] = df_cam["individual"].astype(str).map(ind_to_mid).astype(int)

    # Step 1: prototypes
    if manual_mouse0_bgr is not None and manual_mouse1_bgr is not None:
        proto0_bgr = manual_mouse0_bgr.astype(np.float64)
        proto1_bgr = manual_mouse1_bgr.astype(np.float64)
        print(f"[autoCorrect] Using MANUAL prototypes (BGR): mouse0~{proto0_bgr.round(1).tolist()} mouse1~{proto1_bgr.round(1).tolist()}")
    else:
        sep_frames = _pick_separation_frames(df_cam, min_lik=sep_likelihood, k=calib_frames)
        if len(sep_frames) < 3:
            print("[autoCorrect] Not enough separated frames found; skipping correction.")
            return df_cam.drop(columns=["mid"], errors="ignore")
        proto0_bgr, proto1_bgr = estimate_fur_prototypes_from_paw_cog(
            df_cam=df_cam.drop(columns=["mid"], errors="ignore"),
            video_path=video_path,
            sep_frames=sep_frames,
            patch_radius=patch_radius,
            calib_likelihood=calib_likelihood,
        )
        print(f"[autoCorrect] Estimated prototypes (BGR): mouse0(brown)~{proto0_bgr.round(1).tolist()} mouse1(blue)~{proto1_bgr.round(1).tolist()}")

    # Step 2: per-row color id assignment
    cap = cv2.VideoCapture(str(video_path))
    if not cap.isOpened():
        raise RuntimeError(f"Could not open video for correction: {video_path}")

    df_cam = df_cam.sort_values("frame").reset_index(drop=True)
    frames_arr = df_cam["frame"].to_numpy(dtype=np.int64)
    nrows = len(df_cam)
    df_cam["color_id"] = -1
    df_cam["color_conf"] = 0.0

    idx = 0
    fr = 0
    while True:
        ok, frame = cap.read()
        if not ok:
            break
        while idx < nrows and frames_arr[idx] < fr:
            idx += 1
        start = idx
        while idx < nrows and frames_arr[idx] == fr:
            idx += 1
        if idx > start:
            sub = df_cam.iloc[start:idx]
            for ridx, r in zip(range(start, idx), sub.itertuples(index=False)):
                if float(r.likelihood) < vote_likelihood:
                    continue
                cid, conf = _assign_color_id(
                    frame, float(r.x), float(r.y),
                    patch_radius,
                    proto0_bgr, proto1_bgr,
                    color_dist, min_fur_frac, min_pixels, dominance
                )
                if cid != -1:
                    df_cam.at[ridx, "color_id"] = cid
                    df_cam.at[ridx, "color_conf"] = conf
        fr += 1

    cap.release()

    votes = df_cam[(df_cam["color_id"] >= 0) & (df_cam["likelihood"] >= vote_likelihood)]
    if votes.empty:
        print("[autoCorrect] No usable color votes; skipping correction.")
        return df_cam.drop(columns=["mid"], errors="ignore")

    # Step 3: frame-level swap majority
    def score_frame(x: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:
        mid = x["mid"].to_numpy(dtype=int)
        cid = x["color_id"].to_numpy(dtype=int)
        nos = int(np.sum(cid == mid))
        sw = int(np.sum(cid == (1 - mid)))
        return pd.Series({"noswap": nos, "swap": sw})

    scores = votes.groupby("frame").apply(score_frame).reset_index()
    swap_frames = set(scores[scores["swap"] > scores["noswap"]]["frame"].astype(int).tolist())
    if swap_frames:
        print(f"[autoCorrect] Frame-level swaps: {len(swap_frames)} frames.")

    df_cam["mid_corr"] = df_cam["mid"].astype(int)
    df_cam.loc[df_cam["frame"].isin(swap_frames), "mid_corr"] = 1 - df_cam.loc[df_cam["frame"].isin(swap_frames), "mid_corr"]

    # Step 4: per-bodypart safe move / swap / drop
    keep = np.ones(len(df_cam), dtype=bool)

    for (fr, bp), grp in df_cam.groupby(["frame", "bodypart"]):
        rows = {}
        for mid in (0, 1):
            sub = grp[grp["mid_corr"] == mid]
            if sub.empty:
                continue
            rows[mid] = sub.sort_values("likelihood", ascending=False).iloc[0]
        if not rows:
            continue

        if 0 in rows and 1 in rows:
            r0, r1 = rows[0], rows[1]
            if int(r0["color_id"]) == 1 and int(r1["color_id"]) == 0:
                df_cam.at[r0.name, "mid_corr"] = 1
                df_cam.at[r1.name, "mid_corr"] = 0
                continue

        for mid, r in rows.items():
            cid = int(r["color_id"])
            if cid < 0 or cid == mid:
                continue
            target = cid
            if target not in rows:
                df_cam.at[r.name, "mid_corr"] = target
            else:
                if drop_on_conflict:
                    keep[r.name] = False

    df_cam = df_cam[keep].copy()
    df_cam["individual"] = df_cam["mid_corr"].astype(int).map(lambda m: f"mouse{m}")

    return df_cam.drop(columns=["mid", "mid_corr"], errors="ignore")
"""

v4 = before + new_corr + "\n\n" + after

Assistant: from pathlib import Path
import os, stat

src = Path("/mnt/data/overlay_dlc_on_videos_v3.py").read_text(encoding="utf-8")

start_marker = "# -----------------------------\n# Color-based identity correction (2 mice)\n"
start = src.find(start_marker)
if start == -1:
    raise RuntimeError("Could not find correction section start marker.")
end_marker = "# -----------------------------\n# CLI\n"
end = src.find(end_marker, start)
if end == -1:
    raise RuntimeError("Could not find CLI marker after correction section.")

before = src[:start]
after = src[end:]  # includes CLI and rest

# new correction section as defined earlier (same as in previous attempt)
new_corr = """# -----------------------------
# Color-based identity correction (2 mice)
# -----------------------------
def parse_bgr_triplet(s: str) -> np.ndarray:
    \"\"\"Parse 'b,g,r' or 'b g r' into float64 array shape (3,).\"\"\"
    if s is None:
        raise ValueError("Empty BGR string")
    t = str(s).strip().replace(",", " ").split()
    if len(t) != 3:
        raise ValueError(f"Expected 3 values for BGR, got: {s!r}")
    return np.array([float(t[0]), float(t[1]), float(t[2])], dtype=np.float64)


def _kmeans2(points: np.ndarray, iters: int = 25) -> Tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
    \"\"\"Small kmeans for k=2. Returns (centers (2,3), labels (N,)).\"\"\"
    if len(points) < 2:
        raise ValueError("Need >=2 points for kmeans2")
    pts = points.astype(np.float64)

    # init: farthest pair heuristic
    p0 = pts[0]
    d = np.sum((pts - p0) ** 2, axis=1)
    c1 = pts[int(np.argmax(d))]
    d2 = np.sum((pts - c1) ** 2, axis=1)
    c0 = pts[int(np.argmax(d2))]
    centers = np.stack([c0, c1], axis=0).astype(np.float64)

    labels = np.zeros(len(pts), dtype=np.int32)
    for _ in range(iters):
        dist0 = np.sum((pts - centers[0]) ** 2, axis=1)
        dist1 = np.sum((pts - centers[1]) ** 2, axis=1)
        labels = (dist1 < dist0).astype(np.int32)
        for k in (0, 1):
            sel = pts[labels == k]
            if len(sel) > 0:
                centers[k] = np.mean(sel, axis=0)

    dist0 = np.sum((pts - centers[0]) ** 2, axis=1)
    dist1 = np.sum((pts - centers[1]) ** 2, axis=1)
    labels = (dist1 < dist0).astype(np.int32)
    return centers, labels


def _pick_separation_frames(df_cam: pd.DataFrame, min_lik: float, k: int) -> List[int]:
    \"\"\"Pick frames where the two labeled individuals are far apart (centroid distance).\"\"\"
    d = df_cam[df_cam["likelihood"] >= min_lik].copy()
    if d.empty:
        return []
    inds = sorted(d["individual"].astype(str).unique().tolist())
    if len(inds) != 2:
        return []
    mapping = {inds[0]: 0, inds[1]: 1}
    d["mid_tmp"] = d["individual"].astype(str).map(mapping).astype(int)
    g = d.groupby(["frame", "mid_tmp"])[["x", "y"]].mean().reset_index()
    g0 = g[g["mid_tmp"] == 0].set_index("frame")
    g1 = g[g["mid_tmp"] == 1].set_index("frame")
    frames = sorted(list(set(g0.index).intersection(set(g1.index))))
    if not frames:
        return []
    dist = []
    for fr in frames:
        dx = float(g0.loc[fr, "x"] - g1.loc[fr, "x"])
        dy = float(g0.loc[fr, "y"] - g1.loc[fr, "y"])
        dist.append((int(fr), (dx*dx + dy*dy) ** 0.5))
    dist.sort(key=lambda t: t[1], reverse=True)
    return [fr for fr, _ in dist[:k]]


def _median_patch(frame_bgr: np.ndarray, x: float, y: float, r: int) -> Optional[np.ndarray]:
    if not (np.isfinite(x) and np.isfinite(y)):
        return None
    H, W = frame_bgr.shape[:2]
    xi, yi = int(round(x)), int(round(y))
    x0, x1 = max(0, xi - r), min(W, xi + r + 1)
    y0, y1 = max(0, yi - r), min(H, yi + r + 1)
    patch = frame_bgr[y0:y1, x0:x1]
    if patch.size == 0:
        return None
    pix = patch.reshape(-1, 3).astype(np.float64)
    return np.median(pix, axis=0)


def _assign_color_id(
    frame_bgr: np.ndarray,
    x: float, y: float,
    r: int,
    proto0_bgr: np.ndarray,  # mouse0
    proto1_bgr: np.ndarray,  # mouse1
    dist_thresh: float,
    min_frac: float,
    min_pixels: int,
    dominance: float,
) -> Tuple[int, float]:
    \"\"\"Return (assigned_id in {0,1,-1}, confidence).\"\"\"
    if not (np.isfinite(x) and np.isfinite(y)):
        return -1, 0.0
    H, W = frame_bgr.shape[:2]
    xi, yi = int(round(x)), int(round(y))
    x0, x1 = max(0, xi - r), min(W, xi + r + 1)
    y0, y1 = max(0, yi - r), min(H, yi + r + 1)
    patch = frame_bgr[y0:y1, x0:x1]
    if patch.size == 0:
        return -1, 0.0
    pix = patch.reshape(-1, 3).astype(np.float64)
    n = pix.shape[0]
    if n < min_pixels:
        return -1, 0.0
    thr2 = float(dist_thresh) ** 2
    d0 = np.sum((pix - proto0_bgr) ** 2, axis=1)
    d1 = np.sum((pix - proto1_bgr) ** 2, axis=1)
    c0 = int(np.sum(d0 <= thr2))
    c1 = int(np.sum(d1 <= thr2))
    best = 0 if c0 >= c1 else 1
    bestc = max(c0, c1)
    otherc = min(c0, c1)
    frac = bestc / max(1, n)
    if frac < min_frac:
        return -1, 0.0
    if bestc < otherc * (1.0 + dominance) and (bestc - otherc) < 5:
        return -1, 0.0
    conf = (bestc - otherc) / max(1, n)
    return best, float(conf)


def _paw_centroid(rows: pd.DataFrame, paw_parts: List[str], min_lik: float) -> Optional[Tuple[float, float]]:
    sub = rows[(rows["bodypart"].astype(str).isin(paw_parts)) & (rows["likelihood"] >= min_lik)]
    if len(sub) < 2:
        return None
    return float(sub["x"].mean()), float(sub["y"].mean())


def _fallback_centroid(rows: pd.DataFrame, parts: List[str], min_lik: float) -> Optional[Tuple[float, float]]:
    sub = rows[(rows["bodypart"].astype(str).isin(parts)) & (rows["likelihood"] >= min_lik)]
    if len(sub) < 2:
        return None
    return float(sub["x"].mean()), float(sub["y"].mean())


def estimate_fur_prototypes_from_paw_cog(
    df_cam: pd.DataFrame,
    video_path: str | Path,
    sep_frames: List[int],
    patch_radius: int,
    calib_likelihood: float,
) -> Tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
    \"\"\"
    Returns (mouse0_bgr, mouse1_bgr) using center-of-gravity of paws (or fallback core parts).
    Color samples (BGR) from BOTH labeled individuals are clustered into 2 clusters in color space,
    disregarding IDs. Cluster with larger (R-B) is assigned to mouse0 (brownish), other to mouse1.
    \"\"\"
    paw_parts = ["left_front_paw", "right_front_paw", "left_hind_paw", "right_hind_paw"]
    fallback_parts = ["head", "tail_root", "nose_tip", "left_ear_tip", "right_ear_tip"]

    inds = sorted(df_cam["individual"].astype(str).unique().tolist())
    if len(inds) != 2:
        raise ValueError(f"Expected 2 individuals, got: {inds}")

    df_cam = df_cam.copy()
    df_cam["frame"] = df_cam["frame"].astype(int)

    cap = cv2.VideoCapture(str(video_path))
    if not cap.isOpened():
        raise RuntimeError(f"Could not open video for calibration: {video_path}")

    df_cam = df_cam.sort_values("frame").reset_index(drop=True)
    frames_arr = df_cam["frame"].to_numpy(dtype=np.int64)
    nrows = len(df_cam)
    idx = 0

    sep_set = set(sep_frames)
    max_fr = max(sep_frames) if sep_frames else -1
    samples = []

    fr = 0
    while True:
        ok, frame = cap.read()
        if not ok:
            break
        if max_fr >= 0 and fr > max_fr:
            break

        if fr in sep_set:
            while idx < nrows and frames_arr[idx] < fr:
                idx += 1
            start = idx
            while idx < nrows and frames_arr[idx] == fr:
                idx += 1
            if idx > start:
                rows_fr = df_cam.iloc[start:idx]
                for ind in inds:
                    rows_ind = rows_fr[rows_fr["individual"].astype(str) == ind]
                    cog = _paw_centroid(rows_ind, paw_parts, calib_likelihood)
                    if cog is None:
                        cog = _fallback_centroid(rows_ind, fallback_parts, calib_likelihood)
                    if cog is None:
                        continue
                    c = _median_patch(frame, cog[0], cog[1], patch_radius)
                    if c is not None and np.all(np.isfinite(c)):
                        samples.append(c)

        fr += 1

    cap.release()

    if len(samples) < 20:
        raise RuntimeError("Too few color samples for calibration (need >=20).")

    pts = np.stack(samples, axis=0)
    _, labels = _kmeans2(pts, iters=30)

    protoA = np.median(pts[labels == 0], axis=0)
    protoB = np.median(pts[labels == 1], axis=0)

    if (protoA[2] - protoA[0]) >= (protoB[2] - protoB[0]):
        return protoA.astype(np.float64), protoB.astype(np.float64)
    else:
        return protoB.astype(np.float64), protoA.astype(np.float64)


def correct_identities_for_camera(
    df_cam: pd.DataFrame,
    video_path: str | Path,
    sep_likelihood: float,
    calib_frames: int,
    calib_likelihood: float,
    vote_likelihood: float,
    patch_radius: int,
    color_dist: float,
    min_fur_frac: float,
    min_pixels: int,
    dominance: float,
    drop_on_conflict: bool,
    manual_mouse0_bgr: Optional[np.ndarray] = None,
    manual_mouse1_bgr: Optional[np.ndarray] = None,
) -> pd.DataFrame:
    \"\"\"
    Step 3: per-frame majority check against DLC IDs -> swap mapping if needed.
    Step 4: per-part corrections; if conflict and --drop-on-conflict, drop leaving part.
    \"\"\"
    df_cam = df_cam.copy()
    df_cam["frame"] = df_cam["frame"].astype(int)

    inds = sorted(df_cam["individual"].astype(str).unique().tolist())
    if len(inds) != 2:
        print(f"[autoCorrect] Expected 2 individuals, found {inds}. Skipping correction.")
        return df_cam

    # Only used for comparing to DLC IDs; doesn't assume these correspond to true mouse0/1.
    ind_to_mid = {inds[0]: 0, inds[1]: 1}
    df_cam["mid"] = df_cam["individual"].astype(str).map(ind_to_mid).astype(int)

    # Step 1: prototypes
    if manual_mouse0_bgr is not None and manual_mouse1_bgr is not None:
        proto0_bgr = manual_mouse0_bgr.astype(np.float64)
        proto1_bgr = manual_mouse1_bgr.astype(np.float64)
        print(f"[autoCorrect] Using MANUAL prototypes (BGR): mouse0~{proto0_bgr.round(1).tolist()} mouse1~{proto1_bgr.round(1).tolist()}")
    else:
        sep_frames = _pick_separation_frames(df_cam, min_lik=sep_likelihood, k=calib_frames)
        if len(sep_frames) < 3:
            print("[autoCorrect] Not enough separated frames found; skipping correction.")
            return df_cam.drop(columns=["mid"], errors="ignore")
        proto0_bgr, proto1_bgr = estimate_fur_prototypes_from_paw_cog(
            df_cam=df_cam.drop(columns=["mid"], errors="ignore"),
            video_path=video_path,
            sep_frames=sep_frames,
            patch_radius=patch_radius,
            calib_likelihood=calib_likelihood,
        )
        print(f"[autoCorrect] Estimated prototypes (BGR): mouse0(brownish)~{proto0_bgr.round(1).tolist()} mouse1(blueish)~{proto1_bgr.round(1).tolist()}")

    # Step 2: assign color_id per row
    cap = cv2.VideoCapture(str(video_path))
    if not cap.isOpened():
        raise RuntimeError(f"Could not open video for correction: {video_path}")

    df_cam = df_cam.sort_values("frame").reset_index(drop=True)
    frames_arr = df_cam["frame"].to_numpy(dtype=np.int64)
    nrows = len(df_cam)

    df_cam["color_id"] = -1
    df_cam["color_conf"] = 0.0

    idx = 0
    fr = 0
    while True:
        ok, frame = cap.read()
        if not ok:
            break
        while idx < nrows and frames_arr[idx] < fr:
            idx += 1
        start = idx
        while idx < nrows and frames_arr[idx] == fr:
            idx += 1
        if idx > start:
            sub = df_cam.iloc[start:idx]
            for ridx, r in zip(range(start, idx), sub.itertuples(index=False)):
                if float(r.likelihood) < vote_likelihood:
                    continue
                cid, conf = _assign_color_id(
                    frame, float(r.x), float(r.y),
                    patch_radius,
                    proto0_bgr, proto1_bgr,
                    color_dist, min_fur_frac, min_pixels, dominance
                )
                if cid != -1:
                    df_cam.at[ridx, "color_id"] = cid
                    df_cam.at[ridx, "color_conf"] = conf
        fr += 1

    cap.release()

    votes = df_cam[(df_cam["color_id"] >= 0) & (df_cam["likelihood"] >= vote_likelihood)]
    if votes.empty:
        print("[autoCorrect] No usable color votes; skipping correction.")
        return df_cam.drop(columns=["mid"], errors="ignore")

    # Step 3: frame swap decision
    def score_frame(x: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.Series:
        mid = x["mid"].to_numpy(dtype=int)
        cid = x["color_id"].to_numpy(dtype=int)
        nos = int(np.sum(cid == mid))
        sw = int(np.sum(cid == (1 - mid)))
        return pd.Series({"noswap": nos, "swap": sw})

    scores = votes.groupby("frame").apply(score_frame).reset_index()
    swap_frames = set(scores[scores["swap"] > scores["noswap"]]["frame"].astype(int).tolist())
    if swap_frames:
        print(f"[autoCorrect] Frame-level swaps: {len(swap_frames)} frames.")

    df_cam["mid_corr"] = df_cam["mid"].astype(int)
    m = df_cam["frame"].isin(swap_frames)
    df_cam.loc[m, "mid_corr"] = 1 - df_cam.loc[m, "mid_corr"]

    # Step 4: per-bodypart correction
    keep = np.ones(len(df_cam), dtype=bool)
    for (fr, bp), grp in df_cam.groupby(["frame", "bodypart"]):
        rows = {}
        for mid in (0, 1):
            sub = grp[grp["mid_corr"] == mid]
            if sub.empty:
                continue
            rows[mid] = sub.sort_values("likelihood", ascending=False).iloc[0]
        if not rows:
            continue

        if 0 in rows and 1 in rows:
            r0, r1 = rows[0], rows[1]
            if int(r0["color_id"]) == 1 and int(r1["color_id"]) == 0:
                df_cam.at[r0.name, "mid_corr"] = 1
                df_cam.at[r1.name, "mid_corr"] = 0
                continue

        for mid, r in rows.items():
            cid = int(r["color_id"])
            if cid < 0 or cid == mid:
                continue
            target = cid
            if target not in rows:
                df_cam.at[r.name, "mid_corr"] = target
            else:
                if drop_on_conflict:
                    keep[r.name] = False

    df_cam = df_cam[keep].copy()
    df_cam["individual"] = df_cam["mid_corr"].astype(int).map(lambda m: f"mouse{m}")

    return df_cam.drop(columns=["mid", "mid_corr"], errors="ignore")
"""

v4 = before + new_corr + "\n\n" + after

# Add CLI args for manual bgr: insert near other autocorrect args. We'll just append near the end of build_arg_parser.
# Find where autocorrect args are defined; in v3 they exist.
insertion_point = '    p.add_argument("--drop-on-conflict", action="store_true",\n'
idx = v4.find(insertion_point)
if idx == -1:
    raise RuntimeError("Could not locate drop-on-conflict arg.")
# find end of that argument block (next blank line after it)
endblock = v4.find("\n\n", idx)
insert_at = endblock + 2
manual_args = (
    '    p.add_argument("--mouse0-bgr", default=None,\n'
    '                   help="Manual BGR prototype for mouse0, format: \'b,g,r\'. Use with --mouse1-bgr.")\n'
    '    p.add_argument("--mouse1-bgr", default=None,\n'
    '                   help="Manual BGR prototype for mouse1, format: \'b,g,r\'. Use with --mouse0-bgr.")\n\n'
)
v4 = v4[:insert_at] + manual_args + v4[insert_at:]

# In main, after rows-per-view print, parse manual
rows_line = '    print(f"Rows per view: top={len(df_top)}, front={len(df_front)}, side={len(df_side)}")\n'
idx2 = v4.find(rows_line)
if idx2 == -1:
    raise RuntimeError("Could not locate rows-per-view print line.")
insert_manual = (
    '    manual0 = manual1 = None\n'
    '    if args.mouse0_bgr is not None or args.mouse1_bgr is not None:\n'
    '        if args.mouse0_bgr is None or args.mouse1_bgr is None:\n'
    '            raise ValueError("Provide both --mouse0-bgr and --mouse1-bgr to use manual prototypes.")\n'
    '        manual0 = parse_bgr_triplet(args.mouse0_bgr)\n'
    '        manual1 = parse_bgr_triplet(args.mouse1_bgr)\n'
)
v4 = v4.replace(rows_line, rows_line + insert_manual)

# Pass manuals into correct_identities_for_camera calls: add kwargs before closing )
v4 = v4.replace('            drop_on_conflict=bool(args.drop_on_conflict),\n        )',
                '            drop_on_conflict=bool(args.drop_on_conflict),\n'
                '            manual_mouse0_bgr=manual0,\n'
                '            manual_mouse1_bgr=manual1,\n'
                '        )')

out_path = Path("/mnt/data/overlay_dlc_on_videos_v4.py")
out_path.write_text(v4, encoding="utf-8")
os.chmod(out_path, os.stat(out_path).st_mode | stat.S_IEXEC)

Assistant: Implemented as **overlay_dlc_on_videos_v4.py** with both requested upgrades:

1) **Manual fur prototypes**
- New CLI options:
  - `--mouse0-bgr "b,g,r"`
  - `--mouse1-bgr "b,g,r"`
- If both are provided, the program **skips automatic color calibration** and uses these prototypes directly.

2) **New automatic prototype estimation (paw COG → cluster in color space ignoring IDs)**
- Instead of sampling around arbitrary bodyparts (which easily hits background), the auto-calibration now:
  - finds frames where the two labeled “individuals” are far apart (separation frames)
  - for each separation frame and each labeled individual:
    - computes the **center of gravity of the paws** (using ≥2 paws with high likelihood)
    - samples the **median patch color** around that COG
    - (fallback: if paws are insufficient, it uses a centroid of core parts like head/tail_root/ears)
  - clusters **all these COG-colors** into **two clusters in BGR space**, **ignoring IDs**
  - computes **prototype colors as channel-wise medians** of cluster members (robust)
  - assigns the cluster with higher `(R-B)` as **mouse0 (brownish)** and the other as **mouse1 (blueish)**

Everything else (frame-level majority swap + safe part-level moves + conflict drop option) remains.

[Download overlay_dlc_on_videos_v4.py](sandbox:/mnt/data/overlay_dlc_on_videos_v4.py)

---

## How to use

### A) Manual prototypes (recommended to debug quickly)
```bash
python overlay_dlc_on_videos_v4.py \
  --dlc ../dlc_long.csv \
  --topIn top.mp4 --frontIn front.mp4 --sideIn side.mp4 \
  --topOut top_anno.mp4 --frontOut front_anno.mp4 --sideOut side_anno.mp4 \
  --joinedVideo joined_anno.mp4 \
  --template ../mouse3_mesh_shortTail.txt \
  --likelihood-min 0.2 \
  --autoCorrect --drop-on-conflict \
  --mouse0-bgr "60,80,140" \
  --mouse1-bgr "140,80,60" \
  --dlcOut ../dlc_long_corrected.csv
```
(Replace those example numbers with your measured prototypes.)

### B) Automatic prototypes (new paw-COG clustering method)
```bash
python overlay_dlc_on_videos_v4.py \
  --dlc ../dlc_long.csv \
  --topIn top.mp4 --frontIn front.mp4 --sideIn side.mp4 \
  --topOut top_anno.mp4 --frontOut front_anno.mp4 --sideOut side_anno.mp4 \
  --joinedVideo joined_anno.mp4 \
  --template ../mouse3_mesh_shortTail.txt \
  --likelihood-min 0.2 \
  --autoCorrect --drop-on-conflict \
  --dlcOut ../dlc_long_corrected.csv
```

## Notes on knobs (if calibration is still unstable)
- `--calib-likelihood` (default 0.85): increase to 0.9 if you still hit background.
- `--patch-radius` (default 6): increase to 8–10 for more stable median color.
- `--color-dist` and `--min-fur-frac`: control how strict the “fur pixel” decision is.

import os, stat, textwrap

v4 = Path("/mnt/data/overlay_dlc_on_videos_v4.py").read_text(encoding="utf-8")

# We'll create v5 with SAM segmentation overlay.
code = v4

# Add SAM imports guarded near top after existing imports.
# Find "import cv2" line and insert after it.
insert_point = "import cv2\n"
sam_imports = """
# Optional: Segment Anything (SAM) for segmentation-based visualization
# Install per official repo: pip install git+https://github.com/facebookresearch/segment-anything.git
try:
    import torch  # type: ignore
    from segment_anything import sam_model_registry, SamPredictor  # type: ignore
    _HAS_SAM = True
except Exception:
    _HAS_SAM = False
"""
code = code.replace(insert_point, insert_point + sam_imports)

# Add helper functions for SAM before CLI marker.
marker = "# -----------------------------\n# CLI\n"
pos = code.find(marker)
assert pos != -1

sam_helpers = r"""
# -----------------------------
# SAM helpers (segmentation visualization)
# -----------------------------
def _kmeans2_xy(points_xy: np.ndarray, iters: int = 20) -> Tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
    """
    KMeans k=2 in 2D. Returns (centers (2,2), labels (N,))
    """
    if len(points_xy) < 2:
        raise ValueError("Need >=2 points for kmeans2_xy")
    pts = points_xy.astype(np.float64)
    p0 = pts[0]
    d = np.sum((pts - p0) ** 2, axis=1)
    c1 = pts[int(np.argmax(d))]
    d2 = np.sum((pts - c1) ** 2, axis=1)
    c0 = pts[int(np.argmax(d2))]
    centers = np.stack([c0, c1], axis=0).astype(np.float64)

    labels = np.zeros(len(pts), dtype=np.int32)
    for _ in range(iters):
        dist0 = np.sum((pts - centers[0]) ** 2, axis=1)
        dist1 = np.sum((pts - centers[1]) ** 2, axis=1)
        labels = (dist1 < dist0).astype(np.int32)
        for k in (0, 1):
            sel = pts[labels == k]
            if len(sel) > 0:
                centers[k] = np.mean(sel, axis=0)

    dist0 = np.sum((pts - centers[0]) ** 2, axis=1)
    dist1 = np.sum((pts - centers[1]) ** 2, axis=1)
    labels = (dist1 < dist0).astype(np.int32)
    return centers, labels


def _two_mouse_prompts_from_rows(
    rows: pd.DataFrame,
    min_lik: float,
    use_dlc_ids: bool,
) -> Optional[np.ndarray]:
    """
    Return point prompts (2,2) in pixel coords (x,y) for the two mice.
    If use_dlc_ids: use current 'individual' labels and compute centroids.
    Else: ignore ids and kmeans-cluster all points into two clusters.
    """
    rows = rows[rows["likelihood"] >= min_lik]
    if len(rows) < 4:
        return None

    if use_dlc_ids:
        inds = sorted(rows["individual"].astype(str).unique().tolist())
        if len(inds) < 2:
            return None
        # take first 2 unique
        inds = inds[:2]
        c = []
        for ind in inds:
            sub = rows[rows["individual"].astype(str) == ind]
            if len(sub) < 2:
                return None
            c.append([float(sub["x"].mean()), float(sub["y"].mean())])
        return np.array(c, dtype=np.float32)

    # kmeans in xy
    pts = rows[["x", "y"]].to_numpy(dtype=np.float64)
    try:
        centers, _ = _kmeans2_xy(pts, iters=25)
    except Exception:
        return None
    return centers.astype(np.float32)


def _sam_load_predictor(checkpoint: str, model_type: str, device: str) -> "SamPredictor":
    if not _HAS_SAM:
        raise RuntimeError(
            "segment_anything/torch not available. Install per https://github.com/facebookresearch/segment-anything "
            "and ensure torch is installed."
        )
    if device == "auto":
        device = "cuda" if torch.cuda.is_available() else "cpu"
    sam = sam_model_registry[model_type](checkpoint=checkpoint)
    sam.to(device=device)
    predictor = SamPredictor(sam)
    return predictor


def _sam_segment_two_mice(
    predictor: "SamPredictor",
    frame_bgr: np.ndarray,
    prompts_xy: np.ndarray,   # (2,2) float32 in xy
    multimask: bool = True,
) -> Tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
    """
    Returns (mask0, mask1) as bool arrays shape (H,W).
    """
    img_rgb = cv2.cvtColor(frame_bgr, cv2.COLOR_BGR2RGB)
    predictor.set_image(img_rgb)

    masks_out = []
    for i in range(2):
        p = prompts_xy[i].reshape(1, 2)
        labels = np.array([1], dtype=np.int32)  # foreground
        masks, scores, _ = predictor.predict(
            point_coords=p,
            point_labels=labels,
            multimask_output=bool(multimask),
        )
        # choose best by score
        best = int(np.argmax(scores))
        masks_out.append(masks[best].astype(bool))

    return masks_out[0], masks_out[1]


def _overlay_masks_constant_color(
    frame_bgr: np.ndarray,
    mask0: np.ndarray,
    mask1: np.ndarray,
    alpha: float,
) -> np.ndarray:
    """
    Replace each mask region with its average color (computed from original frame),
    and alpha-blend onto the original.
    """
    out = frame_bgr.copy().astype(np.float32)

    def apply(mask: np.ndarray):
        nonlocal out
        if mask is None or mask.sum() == 0:
            return
        pix = frame_bgr[mask]
        if pix.size == 0:
            return
        mean_col = pix.reshape(-1, 3).mean(axis=0).astype(np.float32)  # BGR
        seg = out.copy()
        seg_mask = mask.astype(bool)
        seg[seg_mask] = mean_col
        out = (1.0 - alpha) * out + alpha * seg

    # resolve overlaps by assigning overlap to whichever mask is larger (simple heuristic)
    overlap = mask0 & mask1
    if overlap.any():
        if mask0.sum() >= mask1.sum():
            mask1 = mask1 & (~overlap)
        else:
            mask0 = mask0 & (~overlap)

    apply(mask0)
    apply(mask1)
    return np.clip(out, 0, 255).astype(np.uint8)


def overlay_video_with_sam(
    in_path: str | Path,
    out_path: str | Path,
    df_cam: pd.DataFrame,
    edges: Optional[List[Tuple[str, str]]],
    likelihood_min_draw: float,
    draw_labels: bool,
    label_scale: float,
    label_thickness: int,
    force_fps: Optional[float],
    # SAM
    sam_checkpoint: str,
    sam_model_type: str,
    sam_device: str,
    sam_alpha: float,
    sam_min_lik: float,
    sam_use_dlc_ids: bool,
    sam_every: int,
    sam_only: bool,
) -> None:
    """
    Overlays SAM-based two-mouse segmentation (prompted by DLC centroids) and writes video.
    The segmentation visualization fills each mouse mask with its mean color and blends.
    """
    predictor = _sam_load_predictor(sam_checkpoint, sam_model_type, sam_device)

    cap = cv2.VideoCapture(str(in_path))
    if not cap.isOpened():
        raise RuntimeError(f"Could not open input video: {in_path}")

    w = int(cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FRAME_WIDTH))
    h = int(cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FRAME_HEIGHT))
    fps_in = float(cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FPS))
    fps = float(force_fps) if force_fps is not None else (fps_in if fps_in > 1e-6 else 10.0)

    fourcc = cv2.VideoWriter_fourcc(*"mp4v")
    writer = cv2.VideoWriter(str(out_path), fourcc, fps, (w, h))
    if not writer.isOpened():
        raise RuntimeError(f"Could not open output video: {out_path}")

    df_cam = df_cam.sort_values("frame").reset_index(drop=True)
    frames_arr = df_cam["frame"].to_numpy(dtype=np.int64)
    nrows = len(df_cam)
    idx = 0

    # keep last prompts to survive sparse detections
    last_prompts = None

    frame_idx = 0
    while True:
        ok, frame = cap.read()
        if not ok:
            break

        while idx < nrows and frames_arr[idx] < frame_idx:
            idx += 1
        start = idx
        while idx < nrows and frames_arr[idx] == frame_idx:
            idx += 1

        rows = df_cam.iloc[start:idx] if idx > start else df_cam.iloc[0:0]

        do_sam = (sam_every <= 1) or (frame_idx % sam_every == 0)
        out_frame = frame

        if do_sam:
            prompts = _two_mouse_prompts_from_rows(rows, min_lik=sam_min_lik, use_dlc_ids=sam_use_dlc_ids)
            if prompts is None:
                prompts = last_prompts
            else:
                last_prompts = prompts

            if prompts is not None:
                try:
                    m0, m1 = _sam_segment_two_mice(predictor, out_frame, prompts_xy=prompts, multimask=True)
                    out_frame = _overlay_masks_constant_color(out_frame, m0, m1, alpha=float(sam_alpha))
                    # optionally draw prompt points for debugging
                    cv2.circle(out_frame, (int(prompts[0,0]), int(prompts[0,1])), 4, (255,255,255), -1, cv2.LINE_AA)
                    cv2.circle(out_frame, (int(prompts[1,0]), int(prompts[1,1])), 4, (80,220,80), -1, cv2.LINE_AA)
                except Exception:
                    # If SAM fails on a frame, fall back silently
                    pass

        if not sam_only:
            out_frame = overlay_frame(out_frame, rows, edges, likelihood_min_draw, draw_labels, label_scale, label_thickness)

        writer.write(out_frame)
        frame_idx += 1

    cap.release()
    writer.release()


def join_quadrants_from_videos(
    top_video: str | Path,
    front_video: str | Path,
    side_video: str | Path,
    joined_out: str | Path,
    force_fps: Optional[float],
) -> None:
    """
    Create joined mosaic from three already-rendered videos (top/right, side/bottom-left, front/bottom-right).
    Downsampling uses INTER_AREA to avoid aliasing.
    """
    cap_t = cv2.VideoCapture(str(top_video))
    cap_f = cv2.VideoCapture(str(front_video))
    cap_s = cv2.VideoCapture(str(side_video))
    if not cap_t.isOpened() or not cap_f.isOpened() or not cap_s.isOpened():
        raise RuntimeError("Could not open one of the annotated videos for joining.")

    w = int(cap_t.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FRAME_WIDTH))
    h = int(cap_t.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FRAME_HEIGHT))
    fps_in = float(cap_t.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FPS))
    fps = float(force_fps) if force_fps is not None else (fps_in if fps_in > 1e-6 else 10.0)

    w_left = w // 2
    w_right = w - w_left
    h_top = h // 2
    h_bottom = h - h_top

    fourcc = cv2.VideoWriter_fourcc(*"mp4v")
    writer = cv2.VideoWriter(str(joined_out), fourcc, fps, (w, h))
    if not writer.isOpened():
        raise RuntimeError(f"Could not open joined output video: {joined_out}")

    while True:
        ok_t, ft = cap_t.read()
        ok_f, ff = cap_f.read()
        ok_s, fs = cap_s.read()
        if not (ok_t and ok_f and ok_s):
            break

        # normalize if sizes differ
        if ff.shape[1] != w or ff.shape[0] != h:
            ff = cv2.resize(ff, (w, h), interpolation=cv2.INTER_LINEAR)
        if fs.shape[1] != w or fs.shape[0] != h:
            fs = cv2.resize(fs, (w, h), interpolation=cv2.INTER_LINEAR)

        top_small = cv2.resize(ft, (w_right, h_top), interpolation=cv2.INTER_AREA)
        front_small = cv2.resize(ff, (w_right, h_bottom), interpolation=cv2.INTER_AREA)
        side_small = cv2.resize(fs, (w_left, h_bottom), interpolation=cv2.INTER_AREA)

        canvas = np.zeros((h, w, 3), dtype=np.uint8)
        canvas[0:h_top, w_left:w] = top_small
        canvas[h_top:h, 0:w_left] = side_small
        canvas[h_top:h, w_left:w] = front_small
        writer.write(canvas)

    cap_t.release()
    cap_f.release()
    cap_s.release()
    writer.release()
"""
code = code[:pos] + sam_helpers + "\n" + code[pos:]

# Add CLI args for SAM in build_arg_parser. We locate "--force-fps" and insert after.
force_arg = '    p.add_argument("--force-fps", type=float, default=None, help="Override output FPS (else use input video FPS)")\n'
if force_arg not in code:
    raise RuntimeError("Could not locate force-fps arg.")
sam_cli = (
    '\n    # SAM segmentation visualization\n'
    '    p.add_argument("--sam", action="store_true", help="Overlay Segment-Anything (SAM) two-mouse segments (debug/visualization).")\n'
    '    p.add_argument("--sam-checkpoint", default=None, help="Path to SAM checkpoint .pth (required if --sam).")\n'
    '    p.add_argument("--sam-model-type", default="vit_b", help="SAM model type: vit_b, vit_l, vit_h (default vit_b).")\n'
    '    p.add_argument("--sam-device", default="auto", help="Device for SAM: auto, cpu, cuda (default auto).")\n'
    '    p.add_argument("--sam-alpha", type=float, default=0.65, help="Alpha blend for constant-color masks (default 0.65).")\n'
    '    p.add_argument("--sam-min-likelihood", type=float, default=0.5, help="Min DLC likelihood for centroid prompts (default 0.5).")\n'
    '    p.add_argument("--sam-use-dlc-ids", action="store_true", help="Use DLC individual IDs to compute prompts instead of XY kmeans clustering.")\n'
    '    p.add_argument("--sam-every", type=int, default=1, help="Run SAM every N frames (default 1).")\n'
    '    p.add_argument("--sam-only", action="store_true", help="If set, render only SAM segments (no skeleton/points).")\n'
)
code = code.replace(force_arg, force_arg + sam_cli)

# In main: if args.sam, use overlay_video_with_sam instead of overlay_video.
# Find the three overlay calls and replace with conditional.
# We'll locate the "Annotating top video..." blocks and modify.

def replace_overlay_block(view_name, in_arg, out_arg, df_var):
    # return code block string
    return f'''    print("Annotating {view_name} video...")
    if args.sam:
        if args.sam_checkpoint is None:
            raise ValueError("--sam-checkpoint is required when using --sam.")
        overlay_video_with_sam(
            {in_arg}, {out_arg}, {df_var},
            edges=edges,
            likelihood_min_draw=args.likelihood_min,
            draw_labels=args.draw_labels,
            label_scale=args.label_scale,
            label_thickness=args.label_thickness,
            force_fps=args.force_fps,
            sam_checkpoint=args.sam_checkpoint,
            sam_model_type=args.sam_model_type,
            sam_device=args.sam_device,
            sam_alpha=args.sam_alpha,
            sam_min_lik=args.sam_min_likelihood,
            sam_use_dlc_ids=bool(args.sam_use_dlc_ids),
            sam_every=int(args.sam_every),
            sam_only=bool(args.sam_only),
        )
    else:
        overlay_video(
            {in_arg}, {out_arg}, {df_var},
            edges=edges,
            likelihood_min=args.likelihood_min,
            draw_labels=args.draw_labels,
            label_scale=args.label_scale,
            label_thickness=args.label_thickness,
            force_fps=args.force_fps,
        )
    print(f"Wrote: {{{out_arg}}}")'''

# We need to patch exact blocks. We'll use simple replacements for three occurrences "Annotating top video..."
import re
# Replace top block
code = re.sub(
    r'    print\("Annotating top video\.\.\."\)\n    overlay_video\([^\)]*\)\n    print\(f"Wrote: \{args\.topOut\}"\)\n',

)

    code,

# SAM helpers (segmentation visualization)
# -----------------------------
def _kmeans2_xy(points_xy: np.ndarray, iters: int = 20) -> Tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
    """KMeans k=2 in 2D. Returns (centers (2,2), labels (N,))."""
    if len(points_xy) < 2:
        raise ValueError("Need >=2 points for kmeans2_xy")
    pts = points_xy.astype(np.float64)
    p0 = pts[0]
    d = np.sum((pts - p0) ** 2, axis=1)
    c1 = pts[int(np.argmax(d))]

    c0 = pts[int(np.argmax(d2))]
    centers = np.stack([c0, c1], axis=0).astype(np.float64)

    labels = np.zeros(len(pts), dtype=np.int32)
    for _ in range(iters):
